parāśara uvāca

svargāpavargavyāsedhakāraṇaṃ paramarṣayaḥ

pulastya uvāca
vaire mahati yad vākyād guror asyāśritā kṣamā

purāṇasaṃhitākartā bhavān vatsa bhaviṣyati 
devatāpāramārthyaṃ ca yathāvad vetsyate bhavān  ViP

matprasādād asaṃdigdhā tava vatsa bhaviṣyati  ViP

pulastyena yad uktaṃ te sarvam etad bhaviṣyati  ViP

M ins

parāśara uvāca
avikārāya śuddhāya nityāya paramātmane 
sadaikarūparūpāya viṣṇave sarvajiṣṇave  ViP 
namo hiraṇyagarbhāya haraye śaṃkarāya ca

ādhārabhūtaṃ viśvasyāpy aṇīyāṃsam aṇīyasām

jñānasvarūpam atyantanirmalaṃ paramārthataḥ 
tam evārthasvarūpeṇa bhrāntidarśanataḥ sthitam  ViP 
viṣṇuṃ grasiṣṇuṃ viśvasya sthitisarge tathā prabhum 
praṇamya jagatām īśam ajam akṣayam avyayam  ViP 
kathayāmi yathāpūrvaṃ dakṣādyair munisattamaiḥ 
pṛṣṭaḥ provāca bhagavān abjayoniḥ pitāmahaḥ  ViP 
taiś coktaṃ purukutsāya bhūbhuje narmadātaṭe 
sārasvatāya tenāpi mama sārasvatena ca  ViP 
paraḥ parāṇāṃ paramaḥ paramātmātmasaṃsthitaḥ 
rūpavarṇādinirdeśaviśeṣaṇavivarjitaḥ  ViP 
apakṣayavināśābhyāṃ pariṇāmarddhijanmabhiḥ 
varjitaḥ śakyate vaktuṃ yaḥ sadāstīti kevalam  ViP 
sarvatrāsau samastaṃ ca vasaty atreti vai yataḥ 
tataḥ sa vāsudeveti vidvadbhiḥ paripaṭhyate  ViP 
tad brahma paramaṃ nityam ajam akṣayam avyayam 
ekasvarūpaṃ ca sadā heyābhāvāc ca nirmalam  ViP 
tad eva sarvam evaitad vyaktāvyaktasvarūpavat 
tathā puruṣarūpeṇa kālarūpeṇa ca sthitam  ViP 
parasya brahmaṇo rūpaṃ puruṣaḥ prathamaṃ dvija 
vyaktāvyakte tathaivānye rūpe kālas tathāparam  ViP 
pradhānapuruṣavyaktakālānāṃ paramaṃ hi yat 
paśyanti sūrayaḥ śuddhaṃ tad viṣṇoḥ paramaṃ padam  ViP 
pradhānapuruṣavyaktakālās tu pravibhāgaśaḥ 
rūpāṇi sthitisargāntavyaktisadbhāvahetavaḥ  ViP 
vyaktaṃ viṣṇus tathāvyaktaṃ puruṣaḥ kāla eva ca 
krīḍato bālakasyeva ceṣṭāṃ tasya niśāmaya  ViP 
avyaktaṃ kāraṇaṃ yat tat pradhānam ṛṣisattamaiḥ 
procyate prakṛtiḥ sūkṣmā nityā sadasadātmikā  ViP 
akṣayaṃ nānyadādhāram ameyam ajaraṃ dhruvam 
śabdasparśavihīnaṃ tad rūpādibhir asaṃhatam  ViP 
triguṇaṃ taj jagadyonir anādiprabhavāvyayam 
tenāgre sarvam evāsīd vyāptaṃ vai pralayād anu  ViP 
vedavādavido vidvan niyatā brahmavādinaḥ 
paṭhanti caitam evārthaṃ pradhānapratipādakam  ViP 
nāho na rātrir na nabho na bhūmir nāsīt tamo jyotir abhūn na cānyat 
śrotrādibuddhyānupalabhyam ekaṃ prādhānikaṃ brahma pumāṃs tadāsīt  ViP 
viṣṇoḥ svarūpāt parato hi te 'nye rūpe pradhānaṃ puruṣaś ca vipra 
tasyaiva te 'nyena dhṛte viyukte rūpāntaraṃ tad dvija kālasaṃjñam  ViP 
prakṛtau ca sthitaṃ vyaktam atītapralaye tu yat 
tasmāt prākṛtasaṃjño 'yam ucyate pratisaṃcaraḥ  ViP

kālasvarūpaṃ tad viṣṇor maitreya parivartate  ViP

tatas tat paramaṃ brahma paramātmā jaganmayaḥ 
sarvagaḥ sarvabhūteśaḥ sarvātmā parameśvaraḥ  ViP

sa saṃjñāṃ yāti bhagavān eka eva janārdanaḥ  ViP 
sraṣṭā sṛjati cātmānaṃ viṣṇuḥ pālyaṃ ca pāti ca 
upasaṃharate cānte saṃhartā ca svayaṃ prabhuḥ  ViP 
pṛthivy āpas tathā tejo vāyur ākāśam eva ca 
sarvendriyāntaḥkaraṇaṃ puruṣākhyaṃ hi yaj jagat  ViP 
sa eva sarvabhūteśo viśvarūpo yato 'vyayaḥ 
sargādikaṃ tato 'syaiva bhūtastham upakārakam  ViP 
sa eva sṛjyaḥ sa ca sargakartā sa eva pāty atti ca pālyate ca 
brahmādyavasthābhir aśeṣamūrtir viṣṇur variṣṭho varado vareṇyaḥ  ViP 
iti śrīviṣṇupurāṇe prathame 'ṃśe dvitīyo 'dhyāyaḥ 
maitreya uvāca
nirguṇasyāprameyasya śuddhasyāpy amalātmanaḥ 
kathaṃ sargādikartṛtvaṃ brahmaṇo 'bhyupagamyate  ViP 
parāśara uvāca
śaktayaḥ sarvabhāvānām acintyajñānagocarāḥ 
yato 'to brahmaṇas tās tu sargādyā bhāvaśaktayaḥ 
bhavanti tapatāṃ śreṣṭha pāvakasya yathoṣṇatā  ViP 
tan nibodha yathā sarge bhagavān saṃpravartate 
nārāyaṇākhyo bhagavān brahmā lokapitāmahaḥ  ViP 
utpannaḥ procyate vidvan nitya evopacārataḥ  ViP 
nijena tasya mānena āyur varṣaśataṃ smṛtam 
tat parākhyaṃ tadardhaṃ ca parārdham abhidhīyate  ViP 
kālasvarūpaṃ viṣṇoś ca yan mayoktaṃ tavānagha 
tena tasya nibodha tvaṃ parimāṇopapādanam  ViP 
anyeṣāṃ caiva jantūnāṃ carāṇām acarāś ca ye 
bhūbhūbhṛtsāgarādīnām aśeṣāṇāṃ ca sattama  ViP 
kāṣṭhā pañcadaśākhyātā nimeṣā munisattama 
kāṣṭhātriṃśat kalā triṃśat kalā mauhūrtiko vidhiḥ  ViP 
tāvatsaṃkhyair ahorātraṃ muhūrtair mānuṣaṃ smṛtam 
ahorātrāṇi tāvanti māsaḥ pakṣadvayātmakaḥ  ViP 
taiḥ ṣaḍbhir ayanaṃ varṣaṃ dve 'yane dakṣiṇottare 
ayanaṃ dakṣiṇaṃ rātrir devānām uttaraṃ dinam  ViP 
divyair varṣasahasrais tu kṛtatretādisaṃjñitam 
caturyugaṃ dvādaśabhis tadvibhāgaṃ nibodha me  ViP 
catvāri trīṇi dve caikaṃ kṛtādiṣu yathākramam 
divyābdānāṃ sahasrāṇi yugeṣv āhuḥ purāvidaḥ  ViP 
tatpramāṇaiḥ śataiḥ saṃdhyā pūrvā tatrābhidhīyate 
saṃdhyāṃśakaś ca tattulyo yugasyānantaro hi saḥ  ViP 
saṃdhyāsaṃdhyāṃśayor antar yaḥ kālo munisattama 
yugākhyaḥ sa tu vijñeyaḥ kṛtatretādisaṃjñitaḥ  ViP 
kṛtaṃ tretā dvāparaś ca kaliś caiva caturyugam 
procyate tatsahasraṃ ca brahmaṇo divasaṃ mune  ViP 
brahmaṇo divase brahman manavas tu caturdaśa 
bhavanti parimāṇaṃ ca teṣāṃ kālakṛtaṃ śṛṇu  ViP 
saptarṣayaḥ surāḥ śakro manus tatsūnavo nṛpāḥ 
ekakāle hi sṛjyante saṃhriyante ca pūrvavat  ViP 
caturyugāṇāṃ saṃkhyātā sādhikā hy ekasaptatiḥ 
manvantaraṃ manoḥ kālaḥ surādīnāṃ ca sattama  ViP 
aṣṭau śatasahasrāṇi divyayā saṃkhyayā smṛtam 
dvāpañcāśat tathānyāni sahasrāṇy adhikāni tu  ViP 
triṃśatkoṭyas tu saṃpūrṇāḥ saṃkhyātāḥ saṃkhyayā dvija 
saptaṣaṣṭis tathānyāni niyutāni mahāmune  ViP 
D ins
dvicatvāriṃśatā yukta śatenāpy adhikās tathā  ViP 
divyāhnaḥ pañcasāhasramāsā daśa dināṣṭakam  ViP 
catur yāmā muhūrtau dvāv aṣṭāv api kalās tathā  ViP 
kāṣṭā saptadaśa dvau ca nimeṣau tadanantaram  ViP 
daivasyaikanimeṣasya saptamo bhāga iṣyate  ViP 
mānuṣābdās tu lakṣyāṇi tathāṣṭādaśa tatparam  ViP 
sahasram aṣṭāviṃśatyā yutāś cābdā catuḥśatī  ViP 
caturviṃśed ahorātre yutā māsāś ca ṣaṭ tathā  ViP 
nāḍyo dvādaśa tāvatyaḥ kalāś ca tadanantaram  ViP 
pañcaviṃśati kāṣṭāś ca nimeṣā daśasāyikā  ViP 
viṃśatiś ca sahasrāṇi kālo 'yam adhikaṃ vinā 
manvantarasya saṃkhyeyaṃ mānuṣair vatsarair dvija  ViP 
caturdaśaguṇo hy eṣa kālo brāhmam ahaḥ smṛtam 
brāhmo naimittiko nāma tasyānte pratisaṃcaraḥ  ViP 
tadā hi dahyate sarvaṃ trailokyaṃ bhūrbhuvādikam 
janaṃ prayānti tāpārtā maharlokanivāsinaḥ  ViP 
ekārṇave tu trailokye brahmā nārāyaṇātmakaḥ 
bhogiśayyāgataḥ śete trailokyagrāsabṛṃhitaḥ  ViP 
janasthair yogibhir devaś cintyamāno 'bjasaṃbhavaḥ 
tatpramāṇāṃ hi tāṃ rātriṃ tadante sṛjate punaḥ  ViP 
evaṃ tu brahmaṇo varṣam evaṃ varṣaśataṃ ca yat 
śataṃ hi tasya varṣāṇāṃ paramāyur mahātmanaḥ  ViP 
ekam asya vyatītaṃ tu parārdhaṃ brahmaṇo 'nagha 
tasyānte 'bhūn mahākalpaḥ pādma ity abhiviśrutaḥ  ViP 
dvitīyasya parārdhasya vartamānasya vai dvija 
vārāha iti kalpo 'yaṃ prathamaḥ parikīrtitaḥ  ViP 
iti śrīviṣṇupurāṇe prathame 'ṃśe tṛtīyo 'dhyāyaḥ 
maitreya uvāca
brahmā nārāyaṇākhyo 'sau kalpādau bhagavān yathā 
sasarja sarvabhūtāni tad ācakṣva mahāmune  ViP 
parāśara uvāca
prajāḥ sasarja bhagavān brahmā nārāyaṇātmakaḥ 
prajāpatipatir devo yathā tan me niśāmaya  ViP 
atītakalpāvasāne niśāsuptotthitaḥ prabhuḥ 
sattvodriktas tathā brahmā śūnyaṃ lokam avaikṣata  ViP 
nārāyaṇaḥ paro 'cintyaḥ pareṣām api sa prabhuḥ 
brahmasvarūpī bhagavān anādiḥ sarvasaṃbhavaḥ  ViP 
imaṃ codāharanty atra ślokaṃ nārāyaṇaṃ prati 
brahmasvarūpiṇaṃ devaṃ jagataḥ prabhavāpyayam  ViP 
āpo nārā iti proktā āpo vai narasūnavaḥ 
ayanaṃ tasya tāḥ pūrvaṃ tena nārāyaṇaḥ smṛtaḥ  ViP 
toyāntaḥ sa mahīṃ jñātvā jagaty ekārṇave prabhuḥ 
anumānāt taduddhāraṃ kartukāmaḥ prajāpatiḥ  ViP 
akarot sa tanūm anyāṃ kalpādiṣu yathā purā 
matsyakūrmādikāṃ tadvad vārāhaṃ vapur āsthitaḥ  ViP 
vedayajñamayaṃ rūpam aśeṣajagataḥ sthitau 
sthitaḥ sthirātmā sarvātmā paramātmā prajāpatiḥ  ViP 
janalokagataiḥ siddhaiḥ sanakādyair abhiṣṭutaḥ 
praviveśa tadā toyam ātmādhāro dharādharaḥ  ViP 
nirīkṣya taṃ tadā devī pātālatalam āgatam 
tuṣṭāva praṇatā bhūtvā bhaktinamrā vasuṃdharā  ViP 
pṛthivy uvāca
namas te sarvabhūtāya tubhyaṃ śaṅkhagadādhara 
mām uddharāsmād adya tvaṃ tvatto 'haṃ pūrvam utthitā  ViP 
tvayāham uddhṛtā pūrvaṃ tvanmayāhaṃ janārdana 
tathānyāni ca bhūtāni gaganādīny aśeṣataḥ  ViP 
namas te paramātmātman puruṣātman namo 'stu te 
pradhānavyaktabhūtāya kālabhūtāya te namaḥ  ViP 
tvaṃ kartā sarvabhūtānāṃ tvaṃ pātā tvaṃ vināśakṛt 
sargādiṣu prabho brahmaviṣṇurudrātmarūpadhṛk  ViP 
saṃbhakṣayitvā sakalaṃ jagaty ekārṇavīkṛte 
śeṣe tvam eva govinda cintyamāno manīṣibhiḥ  ViP 
bhavato yat paraṃ rūpaṃ tan na jānāti kaścana 
avatāreṣu yad rūpaṃ tad arcanti divaukasaḥ  ViP 
tvām ārādhya paraṃ brahma yātā muktiṃ mumukṣavaḥ 
vāsudevam anārādhya ko mokṣaṃ samavāpsyati  ViP 
yat kiṃcin manasā grāhyaṃ yad grāhyaṃ cakṣurādibhiḥ 
buddhyā ca yat paricchedyaṃ tad rūpam akhilaṃ tava  ViP 
tvanmayāhaṃ tvadādhārā tvatsṛṣṭā tvām upāśritā 
mādhavīm iti loko 'yam abhidhatte tato hi mām  ViP 
jayākhilajñānamaya jaya sthūlamayāvyaya 
jayānanta jayāvyakta jaya vyaktamaya prabho 
parāparātman viśvātmañ jaya yajñapate 'nagha  ViP 
tvaṃ yajñas tvaṃ vaṣaṭkāras tvam oṃkāras tvam agnayaḥ 
tvaṃ vedās tvaṃ tadaṅgāni tvaṃ yajñapuruṣo hare  ViP 
sūryādayo grahās tārā nakṣatrāṇy akhilāni ca 
mūrtāmūrtam adṛśyaṃ ca dṛśyaṃ ca puruṣottama  ViP 
D ins
tathaiva māyayā sarvaṃ tvatto 'ham iva dṛśyate  ViP 
yac coktaṃ yac ca naivoktaṃ mayātra parameśvara 
tat sarvaṃ tvaṃ namas tubhyaṃ bhūyo bhūyo namo namaḥ  ViP 
parāśara uvāca
evaṃ saṃstūyamānas tu pṛthivyā pṛthivīdharaḥ 
sāmasvaradhvaniḥ śrīmāñ jagarja parighargharam  ViP 
tataḥ samutkṣipya dharāṃ svadaṃṣṭrayā mahāvarāhaḥ sphuṭapadmalocanaḥ 
rasātalād utpalapatrasaṃnibhaḥ samutthito nīla ivācalo mahān  ViP 
uttiṣṭhatā tena mukhānilāhataṃ tatsaṃplavāmbho janalokasaṃśrayān 
sanandanādīn apakalmaṣān munīn cakāra bhūyo 'pi pavitratāspadam  ViP 
prayānti toyāni khurāgravikṣate rasātale 'dhaḥ kṛtaśabdasaṃtatam 
śvāsānilārtāḥ paritaḥ prayānti siddhā jane ye niyataṃ vasanti  ViP 
D ins
nārāyaṇasyāpi tanur viśanti   ViP 
uttiṣṭhatas tasya jalārdrakukṣer mahāvarāhasya mahīṃ vigṛhya 
vidhunvato vedamayaṃ śarīraṃ romāntarasthā munayaḥ stuvanti  ViP 
taṃ tuṣṭuvus toṣaparītacetaso loke jane ye nivasanti yoginaḥ 
sanandanādyā natinamrakandharā dharādharaṃ dhīrataroddhatekṣaṇam  ViP 
jayeśvarāṇāṃ parameśa keśava prabho gadāśaṅkhadharāsicakradhṛk 
prasūtināśasthitihetur īśvaras tvam eva nānyat paramaṃ ca yat padam  ViP 
pādeṣu vedās tava yūpadaṃṣṭra danteṣu yajñāś citayaś ca vaktre 
hutāśajihvo 'si tanūruhāṇi darbhāḥ prabho yajñapumāṃs tvam eva  ViP 
vilocane rātryahanī mahātman sarvāspadaṃ brahma paraṃ śiras te 
sūktāny aśeṣāṇi saṭākalāpo ghrāṇaṃ samastāni havīṃṣi deva  ViP 
sruktuṇḍa sāmasvaradhīranāda prāgvaṃśakāyākhilasatrasaṃdhe 
pūrteṣṭadharmaśravaṇo 'si deva sanātanātman bhagavan prasīda  ViP 
padakramākrāntam anantam ādi sthitaṃ tvam evākṣara viśvamūrte 
viśvasya vidmaḥ parameśvaro 'si prasīda nātho 'si carācarasya  ViP 
daṃṣṭrāgravinyastam aśeṣam etad bhūmaṇḍalaṃ nātha vibhāvyate te 
vigāhataḥ padmavanaṃ vilagnaṃ sarojinīpatram ivoḍhapaṅkam  ViP 
dyāvāpṛthivyor atulaprabhāva yad antaraṃ tad vapuṣā tavaiva 
vyāptaṃ jagad vyāptisamarthadīpte hitāya viśvasya vibho bhava tvam  ViP 
paramārthas tvam evaiko nānyo 'sti jagataḥ pate 
tavaiṣa mahimā yena vyāptam etac carācaram  ViP 
yad etad dṛśyate mūrtam etaj jñānātmanas tava 
bhrāntijñānena paśyanti jagadrūpam ayoginaḥ  ViP 
jñānasvarūpam akhilaṃ jagad etad abuddhayaḥ 
arthasvarūpaṃ paśyanto bhrāmyante mohasaṃplave  ViP 
ye tu jñānavidaḥ śuddhacetasas te 'khilaṃ jagat 
jñānātmakaṃ prapaśyanti tvadrūpaṃ parameśvara  ViP 
prasīda sarvasarvātman bhavāya jagatām imām 
uddharorvīm ameyātmañ śaṃ no dehy abjalocana  ViP 
sattvodrikto 'si bhagavan govinda pṛthivīm imām 
samuddhara bhavāyeśa śaṃ no dehy abjalocana  ViP 
sargapravṛttir bhavato jagatām upakāriṇī 
bhavatv eṣā namas te 'stu śaṃ no dehy abjalocana  ViP 
parāśara uvāca
evaṃ saṃstūyamānas tu paramātmā mahīdharaḥ 
ujjahāra kṣitiṃ kṣipraṃ nyastavāṃś ca mahārṇave  ViP 
tasyopari jalaughasya mahatī naur iva sthitā 
vitatatvāt tu dehasya na mahī yāti saṃplavam  ViP 
tataḥ kṣitiṃ samāṃ kṛtvā pṛthivyāṃ so 'cinod girīn 
yathāvibhāgaṃ bhagavān anādiḥ sarvasaṃbhavaḥ  ViP 
prāksargadagdhān akhilān parvatān pṛthivītale 
amoghena prabhāvena sasarjāmoghavāñchitaḥ  ViP 
bhūvibhāgaṃ tataḥ kṛtvā saptadvīpaṃ yathātatham 
bhūrādyāṃś caturo lokān pūrvavat samakalpayat  ViP 
brahmarūpadharo devas tato 'sau rajasā vṛtaḥ 
cakāra sṛṣṭiṃ bhagavāṃś caturvaktradharo hariḥ  ViP 
nimittamātram evāsau sṛjyānāṃ sargakarmaṇi 
pradhānakāraṇībhūtā yato vai sṛjyaśaktayaḥ  ViP 
nimittamātraṃ muktvaikaṃ nānyat kiṃcid apekṣyate 
nīyate tapatāṃ śreṣṭha svaśaktyā vastu vastutām  ViP 
iti śrīviṣṇupurāṇe prathame 'ṃśe caturtho 'dhyāyaḥ 
maitreya uvāca
yathā sasarja devo 'sau devarṣipitṛdānavān 
manuṣyatiryagvṛkṣādīn bhūvyomasalilaukasaḥ  ViP 
yadguṇaṃ yatsvabhāvaṃ ca yadrūpaṃ ca jagad dvija 
sargādau sṛṣṭavān brahmā tan mamācakṣva vistarāt  ViP 
parāśara uvāca
maitreya kathayāmy eṣa śṛṇuṣva susamāhitaḥ 
yathā sasarja devo 'sau devādīn akhilān vibhuḥ  ViP 
sṛṣṭiṃ cintayatas tasya kalpādiṣu yathā purā 
abuddhipūrvakaḥ sargaḥ prādurbhūtas tamomayaḥ  ViP 
tamo moho mahāmohas tāmisro hy andhasaṃjñitaḥ 
avidyā pañcaparvaiṣā prādurbhūtā mahātmanaḥ  ViP 
pañcadhāvasthitaḥ sargo dhyāyato 'pratibodhavān 
bahir antaś cāprakāśaḥ saṃvṛtātmā nagātmakaḥ  ViP 
mukhyā nagā yataś coktā mukhyasargas tatas tv ayam  ViP 
taṃ dṛṣṭvāsādhakaṃ sargam amanyad aparaṃ punaḥ  ViP 
tasyābhidhyāyataḥ sargaṃ tiryaksroto 'bhyavartata 
yasmāt tiryakpravṛttaḥ sa tiryaksrotas tataḥ smṛtaḥ  ViP 
paśvādayas te vikhyātās tamaḥprāyā hy avedinaḥ 
utpathagrāhiṇaś caiva te 'jñāne jñānamāninaḥ  ViP 
ahaṃkṛtā ahaṃmānā aṣṭāviṃśadvadhātmakāḥ 
antaḥprakāśās te sarve āvṛtāś ca parasparam  ViP 
tam apy asādhakaṃ matvā dhyāyato 'nyas tato 'bhavat 
ūrdhvasrotas tṛtīyas tu sāttvikordhvam avartata  ViP 
te sukhaprītibahulā bahir antaś ca nāvṛtāḥ 
prakāśā bahir antaś ca ūrdhvasrotodbhavāḥ smṛtāḥ  ViP 
tuṣṭyātmakas tṛtīyas tu devasargas tu sa smṛtaḥ 
tasmin sarge 'bhavat prītir niṣpanne brahmaṇas tathā  ViP 
tato 'nyaṃ sa tadā dadhyau sādhakaṃ sargam uttamam 
asādhakāṃs tu tāñ jñātvā mukhyasargādisaṃbhavān  ViP 
tathābhidhyāyatas tasya satyābhidhyāyinas tataḥ 
prādurbhūtas tadāvyaktād arvāksrotas tu sādhakaḥ  ViP 
yasmād arvāg vyavartanta tato 'rvāksrotasas tu te 
te ca prakāśabahulās tamoudriktā rajo'dhikāḥ  ViP 
tasmāt te duḥkhabahulā bhūyo bhūyaś ca kāriṇaḥ 
prakāśā bahir antaś ca manuṣyāḥ sādhakās tu te  ViP 
D ins
pañcamo 'nugrahaḥ sargaḥ sa caturdhā vyavasthitaḥ  ViP 
viparyayeṇa cāśaktyā siddhyā tuṣṭyā tathaiva ca  ViP 
nivṛttaṃ vartamānaṃ ca sarve jānanti vai punaḥ  ViP 
bhūtādikānāṃ bhūtānāṃ ṣaṣṭhaḥ sargaḥ sa ucyate  ViP 
te parigrāhiṇaḥ sarge saṃvibhāganatāḥ sadā  ViP 
krodhanāś cāpy aśīlāś ca jñeyā bhūtādikās tu te  ViP 
ity ete kathitāḥ sargāḥ ṣaḍ atra munisattama 
prathamo mahataḥ sargo vijñeyo brahmaṇas tu saḥ  ViP 
tanmātrāṇāṃ dvitīyaś ca bhūtasargas tu sa smṛtaḥ 
vaikārikas tṛtīyas tu sarga aindriyakaḥ smṛtaḥ  ViP 
ity eṣa prākṛtaḥ sargaḥ saṃbhūto buddhipūrvakaḥ 
mukhyasargaś caturthas tu mukhyā vai sthāvarāḥ smṛtāḥ  ViP 
pañcamas tu ca yaḥ proktas tairyagyonyaḥ sa ucyate 
tatordhvasrotasāṃ ṣaṣṭho devasargas tu sa smṛtaḥ  ViP 
tato 'rvāksrotasāṃ sargaḥ saptamaḥ sa tu mānuṣaḥ  ViP 
aṣṭamo 'nugrahaḥ sargaḥ sāttvikas tāmasaś ca saḥ 
pañcaite vaikṛtāḥ sargāḥ prākṛtās tu trayaḥ smṛtāḥ  ViP 
prākṛto vaikṛtaś caiva kaumāro navamaḥ smṛtaḥ 
ity ete vai samākhyātā nava sargāḥ prajāpateḥ  ViP 
prākṛtā vaikṛtāś caiva jagato mūlahetavaḥ 
sṛjato jagadīśasya kim anyac chrotum icchasi  ViP 
maitreya uvāca
saṃkṣepāt kathitaḥ sargo devādīnāṃ mune tvayā 
vistarāc chrotum icchāmi tvatto munivarottama  ViP 
parāśara uvāca
karmabhir bhāvitāḥ pūrvaiḥ kuśalākuśalais tu tāḥ 
khyātyā tayā hy anirmuktāḥ saṃhāre 'py upasaṃhṛtāḥ  ViP 
sthāvarāntāḥ surādyās tu prajā brahmaṃś caturvidhāḥ 
brahmaṇaḥ kurvataḥ sṛṣṭiṃ jajñire mānasās tu tāḥ  ViP 
tato devāsurapitṝn manuṣyāṃś ca catuṣṭayam 
sisṛkṣur ambhāṃsy etāni svam ātmānam ayūyujat  ViP 
yuktātmanas tamomātrā udriktābhūt prajāpateḥ 
sisṛkṣor jaghanāt pūrvam asurā jajñire tataḥ  ViP 
utsasarja tatas tāṃ tu tamomātrātmikāṃ tanum 
sā tu tyaktā tatas tena maitreyābhūd vibhāvarī  ViP 
sisṛkṣur anyadehasthaḥ prītim āpa tataḥ surāḥ 
sattvodriktāḥ samudbhūtā mukhato brahmaṇo dvija  ViP 
tyaktā sāpi tanus tena sattvaprāyam abhūd dinam 
tato hi balino rātrāv asurā devatā divā  ViP 
sattvamātrātmikām eva tato 'nyāṃ jagṛhe tanum 
pitṛvan manyamānasya pitaras tasya jajñire  ViP

sā cotsṛṣṭābhavat saṃdhyā dinanaktāntarasthitā  ViP 
rajomātrātmikām anyāṃ jagṛhe sa tanuṃ tataḥ 
rajomātrotkaṭā jātā manuṣyā dvijasattama  ViP 
tām apy āśu sa tatyāja tanuṃ sadyaḥ prajāpatiḥ

brahmaṇas tu śarīrāṇi triguṇopāśrayāṇi tu  ViP 
rajomātrātmikām eva tato 'nyāṃ jagṛhe tanum

padbhyāṃ cāśvān samātaṅgān rāsabhān gavayān mṛgān

tadānyān mānasān putrān sadṛśān ātmano 'sṛjat  ViP

nava brahmāṇa ity ete purāṇe niścayaṃ gatāḥ  ViP

kathitas tāmasaḥ sargo brahmaṇas te mahāmune

parāśara uvāca
nityaivaiṣā jaganmātā viṣṇoḥ śrīr anapāyinī

eko vyāpī samaḥ śuddho nirguṇaḥ prakṛteḥ paraḥ 
janmavṛddhyādirahita ātmā sarvagato 'vyayaḥ  ViP 
parajñānamayo 'sadbhir nāmajātyādibhir vibhuḥ 
na yogavān na yukto 'bhūn naiva pārthiva yokṣyati  ViP 
tasyātmaparadeheṣu sato 'py ekamayaṃ hi yat 
vijñānaṃ paramārtho 'sau dvaitino 'tattvadarśinaḥ  ViP 
veṇurandhravibhedena bhedaḥ ṣaḍjādisaṃjñitaḥ 
abhedavyāpino vāyos tathā tasya mahātmanaḥ  ViP 
ekatvaṃ rūpabhedaś ca bāhyakarmapravṛttijaḥ 
devādibhede 'padhvaste nāsty evāvaraṇo hi saḥ  ViP 
iti śrīviṣṇupurāṇe dvitīye 'ṃśe caturdaśo 'dhyāyaḥ 
parāśara uvāca
ity ukte mauninaṃ bhūyaś cintayānaṃ mahīpatim 
pratyuvācātha vipro 'sāv advaitāntargatāṃ kathām  ViP 
brāhmaṇa uvāca
śrūyatāṃ nṛpaśārdūla yad gītam ṛbhuṇā purā 
avabodhaṃ janayatā nidāghasya dvijanmanaḥ  ViP 
ṛbhur nāmābhavat putro brahmaṇaḥ parameṣṭhinaḥ 
vijñātatattvasadbhāvo nisargād eva bhūpate  ViP 
ŚD ins
pramāṇatarkataḥ samyak māne meye 'pi niścite  ViP 
tasya śiṣyo nidāgho 'bhūt pulastyatanayaḥ purā 
prādād aśeṣavijñānaṃ sa tasmai parayā mudā  ViP 
avāptajñānatattvasya na tasyādvaitavāsanām 
sa ṛbhus tarkayām āsa nidāghasya nareśvara  ViP 
devikāyās taṭe vīranagaraṃ nāma vai puram 
samṛddham atiramyaṃ ca pulastyena niveśitam  ViP 
ramyopavanaparyante sa tasmin pārthivottama 
nidāgho nāma yogajña ṛbhuśiṣyo 'vasat purā  ViP 
divye varṣasahasre tu samatīte 'sya tat puram 
jagāma sa ṛbhuḥ śiṣyaṃ nidāgham avalokitum  ViP 
sa tasya vaiśvadevānte dvārālokanagocare 
sthitas tena gṛhītārgho nijaveśmapraveśitaḥ  ViP 
prakṣālitāṅghripāṇiṃ ca kṛtāsanaparigraham 
uvāca sa dvijaśreṣṭho bhujyatām iti sādaram  ViP 
ṛbhur uvāca
bho vipravarya bhoktavyaṃ yad annaṃ bhavato gṛhe 
tat kathyatāṃ kadanneṣu na prītiḥ satataṃ mama  ViP 
nidāgha uvāca
saktuyāvakavāṭyānām apūpānāṃ ca me gṛhe 
yad rocate dvijaśreṣṭha tat tvaṃ bhuṅkṣva yathecchayā  ViP 
ṛbhur uvāca
kadannāni dvijaitāni miṣṭam annaṃ prayaccha me 
saṃyāvapāyasādīni drapsaphāṇitavanti ca  ViP 
nidāgha uvāca
he he śālini madgehe yat kiṃcid atiśobhanam 
bhakṣyopasādhanaṃ miṣṭaṃ tenāsyānnaṃ prasādhaya  ViP 
brāhmaṇa uvāca
ity uktā tena sā patnī miṣṭam annaṃ dvijasya yat 
prasādhitavatī tad vai bhartur vacanagauravāt  ViP 
taṃ bhuktavantam icchāto miṣṭam annaṃ mahāmunim 
nidāghaḥ prāha bhūpāla praśrayāvanataḥ sthitaḥ  ViP 
nidāgha uvāca
api te paramā tṛptir utpannā tuṣṭir eva ca

kvanivāso bhavān vipra kva ca gantuṃ samudyataḥ 
āgamyate ca bhavatā yatas tac ca dvijocyatām  ViP 
ṛbhur uvāca
kṣud yasya tasya bhukte 'nne tṛptir brāhmaṇa jāyate 
na me kṣud abhavat tṛptiṃ kasmān māṃ paripṛcchasi  ViP 
vahninā pārthive dhātau kṣapite kṣutsamudbhavaḥ 
bhavaty ambhasi ca kṣīṇe nṛṇāṃ tṛḍ api jāyate  ViP 
kṣuttṛṣṇe dehadharmākhye na mamaite yato dvija 
tataḥ kṣutsaṃbhavābhāvāt tṛptir asty eva me sadā  ViP 
manasaḥ svasthatā tuṣṭiś cittadharmāv imau dvija 
cetaso yasya tat pṛccha pumān ebhir na yujyate  ViP 
kva nivāsas tavety uktaṃ kva gantāsi ca yat tvayā 
kutaś cāgamyate tatra tritaye 'pi nibodha me  ViP 
pumān sarvagato vyāpī ākāśavad ayaṃ yataḥ 
kutaḥ kutra kva gantāsīty etad apy arthavat katham  ViP 
so 'haṃ gantā na cāgantā naikadeśaniketanaḥ 
tvaṃ cānye ca na ca tvaṃ ca nānye naivāham apy aham  ViP 
mṛṣṭaṃ na mṛṣṭam ity eṣā jijñāsā me kṛtā tava 
kiṃ vakṣyatīti tatrāpi śrūyatāṃ dvijasattama  ViP 
kim asvādv atha vā mṛṣṭaṃ bhuñjato 'nnaṃ dvijottama 
mṛṣṭam eva yadāmṛṣṭaṃ tad evodvegakāraṇam  ViP 
amṛṣṭaṃ jāyate mṛṣṭaṃ mṛṣṭād udvijate janaḥ 
ādimadhyāvasāneṣu kim annaṃ rucikārakam  ViP 
mṛṇmayaṃ hi gṛhaṃ yadvan mṛdā liptaṃ sthiraṃ bhavet 
pārthivo 'yaṃ tathā dehaḥ pārthivaiḥ paramāṇubhiḥ  ViP 
M ins
ālipta āpyāyayataḥ puṃso bhogo 'tra kiṃ kṛtaḥ  ViP 
yavagodhūmamudgādi ghṛtaṃ tailaṃ payo dadhi 
guḍaṃ phalādīni tathā pārthivāḥ paramāṇavaḥ  ViP 
tad etad bhavatā jñātvā mṛṣṭāmṛṣṭavicāri yat 
tan manaḥ samatālambi kāryaṃ sāmyaṃ hi muktaye  ViP 
brāhmaṇa uvāca

naṣṭo mohas tavākarṇya vacāṃsy etāni me dvija  ViP 
ṛbhur uvāca

vāsudevābhidheyasya svarūpaṃ paramātmanaḥ  ViP

brāhmaṇa uvāca

pravivikṣau puraṃ ramyaṃ tenātra sthīyate mayā  ViP 
ṛbhur uvāca

kathyatāṃ me dvijaśreṣṭha tvam abhijño mato mama  ViP

adhirūḍho narendro 'yaṃ parilokas tathetaraḥ  ViP 
ṛbhur uvāca
etau hi gajarājānau yugapad darśitau mama

tat kathyatāṃ mahābhāga viśeṣo bhavatānayoḥ 
jñātum icchāmy ahaṃ ko 'tra gajaḥ ko vā narādhipaḥ  ViP

brāhmaṇa uvāca

avabodhāya te brahman dṛṣṭānto darśito mayā  ViP

brāhmaṇa uvāca

yathācāryasya tena tvāṃ manye prāptam ahaṃ gurum  ViP 
ṛbhur uvāca

brāhmaṇa uvāca
evam uktvā yayau vidvān nidāghaṃ sa ṛbhur guruḥ

maitreya uvāca
kathitā guruṇā samyag bhūsamudrādisaṃsthitiḥ 
sūryādīnāṃ ca saṃsthānaṃ jyotiṣām api vistarāt  ViP 
devādīnāṃ tathā sṛṣṭir ṛṣīṇāṃ cāpi varṇitā

manvantarādhipāṃś caiva śakradevapurogamān 
bhavatā kathitān etāñ śrotum icchāmy ahaṃ guro  ViP 
parāśara uvāca
atītānāgatānīha yāni manvantarāṇi vai 
tāny ahaṃ bhavate samyak kathayāmi yathākramam  ViP 
svāyaṃbhuvo manuḥ pūrvaṃ manuḥ svārociṣas tathā 
uttamas tāmasaś caiva raivataś cākṣuṣas tathā  ViP 
ṣaḍ ete manavo 'tītāḥ sāmprataṃ tu raveḥ sutaḥ 
vaivasvato 'yaṃ yasyaitat saptamaṃ vartate 'ntaram  ViP 
svāyaṃbhuvaṃ tu kathitaṃ kalpādāv antaraṃ mayā 
devās tatrarṣayaś caiva yathāvat kathitā mayā  ViP 
ata ūrdhvaṃ pravakṣyāmi manoḥ svārociṣasya tu 
manvantarādhipān samyag devarṣīṃs tatsutāṃs tathā  ViP 
pārāvatāḥ satuṣitā devāḥ svārociṣe 'ntare 
vipaścit tatra devendro maitreyāsīn mahābalaḥ  ViP 
ūrjaḥ stambhas tathā prāṇo dattolir ṛṣabhas tathā

suśāntir nāma devendro maitreyābhūt sureśvaraḥ  ViP 
sudhāmānas tathā satyāḥ śivāś cāsan pratardanāḥ

vasiṣṭhatanayās tatra sapta saptarṣayo 'bhavan 
ajaḥ paraśudivyādyās tathottamamanoḥ sutāḥ  ViP 
tāmasasyāntare devāḥ surūpā harayas tathā

śibir indras tathā cāsīc śatayajñopalakṣaṇaḥ 
saptarṣayaś ca ye teṣāṃ tatra nāmāni me śṛṇu  ViP

naraḥ khyātiḥ śāntahayo jānujaṅghādayas tathā 
putrās tu tāmasasyāsan rājānaḥ sumahābalāḥ  ViP 
pañcame cāpi maitreya raivato nāma nāmataḥ 
manur vibhuś ca tatrendro devāṃś caivāntare śṛṇu  ViP 
amitābhā bhūtarayā vaikuṇṭhāḥ sasumedhasaḥ 
ete devagaṇās tatra caturdaśa caturdaśa  ViP 
hiraṇyaromā vedaśrīr ūrdhvabāhus tathāparaḥ 
vedabāhuḥ sudhāmā ca parjanyaś ca mahāmuniḥ 
ete saptarṣayo vipra tatrāsan raivate 'ntare  ViP 
balabandhuḥ susaṃbhāvyaḥ satyakādyāś ca tatsutāḥ 
narendrāḥ sumahāvīryā babhūvur munisattama  ViP 
svārociṣaś cottamaś ca tāmaso raivatas tathā

manvantarādhipān etāṃl labdhavān ātmavaṃśajān  ViP

manojavas tathaivendro devān api nibodha me  ViP 
āpyāḥ prasūtā bhavyāś ca pṛthugāś ca divaukasaḥ 
mahānubhāvā lekhāś ca pañcaite hy aṣṭakā gaṇāḥ  ViP 
sumedhā virajāś caiva haviṣmān uttamo madhuḥ 
atināmā sahiṣṇuś ca saptāsann iti carṣayaḥ  ViP 
ūruḥ pūruḥ śatadyumnapramukhāḥ sumahābalāḥ 
cākṣuṣasya manoḥ putrāḥ pṛthivīpatayo 'bhavan  ViP 
vivasvataḥ suto vipra śrāddhadevo mahādyutiḥ 
manuḥ saṃvartate dhīmān sāmprataṃ saptame 'ntare  ViP

puraṃdaras tathaivātra maitreya tridaśeśvaraḥ  ViP

viśvāmitrabharadvājau sapta saptarṣayo 'tra tu  ViP

tāmasasyāntare caiva saṃprāpte punar eva hi

raivate 'py antare devaḥ saṃbhūtyāṃ mānaso 'bhavat

cākṣuṣe cāntare devo vaikuṇṭhaḥ puruṣottamaḥ 
vikuṇṭhāyām asau jajñe vaikuṇṭhair daivataiḥ saha  ViP

tribhiḥ kramair imāṃl lokāñ jitvā yena mahātmanā

sarve ca devā manavaḥ samastāḥ saptarṣayo ye manusūnavaś ca

iti śrīviṣṇupurāṇe tṛtīyāṃśe prathamo 'dhyāyaḥ 
maitreya uvāca
proktāny etāni bhavatā sapta manvantarāṇi vai 
bhaviṣyāṇy api viprarṣe mamākhyātuṃ tvam arhasi  ViP 
parāśara uvāca
sūryasya patnī saṃjñābhūt tanayā viśvakarmaṇaḥ 
manur yamo yamī caiva tadapatyāni vai mune  ViP 
asahantī tu sā bhartus tejaś chāyāṃ yuyoja vai 
bhartuḥ śuśrūṣaṇe 'raṇyaṃ svayaṃ ca tapase yayau  ViP 
saṃjñeyam ity athārkaś ca chāyāyām ātmajatrayam 
śanaiścaraṃ manuṃ cānyaṃ tapatīṃ cāpy ajījanat  ViP 
chāyāsaṃjñā dadau śāpaṃ yamāya kupitā yadā 
tadānyeyam asau buddhir ity āsīd yamasūryayoḥ  ViP 
tato vivasvān ākhyāte tayaivāraṇyasaṃsthitām 
samādhidṛṣṭyā dadṛśe tām aśvāṃ tapasi sthitām  ViP 
vājirūpadharaḥ so 'pi tasyāṃ devāv athāśvinau 
janayām āsa revantaṃ retaso 'nte ca bhāskaraḥ  ViP 
āninye ca punaḥ saṃjñāṃ svasthānaṃ bhagavān raviḥ 
tejasaḥ śamanaṃ cāsya viśvakarmā cakāra ha  ViP 
bhramam āropya sūryaṃ tu tasya tejoviśātanam 
kṛtavān aṣṭamaṃ bhāgaṃ na vyaśātayatāvyayam  ViP 
yat sūryād vaiṣṇavaṃ tejaḥ śātitaṃ viśvakarmaṇā 
jājvalyamānam apatat tad bhūmau munisattama  ViP 
tvaṣṭaiva tejasā tena viṣṇoś cakram akalpayat 
triśūlaṃ caiva śarvasya śibikāṃ dhanadasya ca  ViP 
śaktiṃ guhasya devānām anyeṣāṃ ca yad āyudham 
tat sarvaṃ tejasā tena viśvakarmā vyavardhayat  ViP 
chāyāsaṃjñāsuto yo 'sau dvitīyaḥ kathito manuḥ 
pūrvajasya savarṇo 'sau sāvarṇis tena kathyate  ViP 
tasya manvantaraṃ hy etat sāvarṇikam athāṣṭamam 
tac chṛṇuṣva mahābhāga bhaviṣyaṃ kathayāmi te  ViP 
sāvarṇis tu manur yo 'sau maitreya bhavitā tataḥ 
sutapāś cāmitābhāś ca mukhyāś cāpi tadā surāḥ  ViP 
teṣāṃ gaṇas tu devānām ekaiko viṃśakaḥ smṛtaḥ 
saptarṣīn api vakṣyāmi bhaviṣyān munisattama  ViP 
dīptimān gālavo rāmaḥ kṛpo drauṇis tathāparaḥ 
matputraś ca tathā vyāsa ṛśyaśṛṅgaś ca saptamaḥ  ViP 
viṣṇuprasādād anaghaḥ pātālāntaragocaraḥ 
virocanasutas teṣāṃ balir indro bhaviṣyati  ViP 
virajāś cārvarīvaṃś ca nirmohādyās tathāpare 
sāvarṇes tu manoḥ putrā bhaviṣyanti nareśvarāḥ  ViP 
navamo dakṣasāvarṇir maitreya bhavitā manuḥ  ViP 
pārā marīcigarbhāś ca sudharmāṇas tathā tridhā 
bhaviṣyanti tadā devā ekaiko dvādaśo gaṇaḥ  ViP 
teṣām indro mahāvīryo bhaviṣyaty adbhuto dvija  ViP 
savano dyutimān bhavyo vasur medhātithis tathā 
jyotiṣmān saptamaḥ satyas tatraite ca maharṣayaḥ  ViP 
dhṛtaketur dīptiketuḥ pañcahasto nirāmayaḥ 
pṛthuśravādyāś ca tathā dakṣasāvarṇikātmajāḥ  ViP 
daśamo brahmasāvarṇir bhaviṣyati mune manuḥ 
sudhāmāno viruddhāś ca śatasaṃkhyās tathā surāḥ  ViP 
teṣām indraś ca bhavitā śāntir nāma mahābalaḥ 
saptarṣayo bhaviṣyanti ye tadā tāñ chṛṇuṣva ca  ViP 
haviṣmān sukṛtiḥ satyo hy apāṃmūrtis tathāparaḥ 
nābhāgo 'pratimaujāś ca satyaketus tathaiva ca  ViP 
sukṣetraś cottamaujāś ca bhūriṣeṇādayo daśa 
brahmasāvarṇiputrās tu rakṣiṣyanti vasuṃdharām  ViP 
ekādaśaś ca bhavitā dharmasāvarṇiko manuḥ  ViP 
vihaṃgamāḥ kāmagamā nirmāṇarucayas tathā 
gaṇās tv ete tadā mukhyā devānāṃ ca bhaviṣyatām 
ekaikas triṃśakas teṣāṃ gaṇaś cendraś ca vai vṛṣaḥ  ViP 
niścaraś cāgnitejāś ca vapuṣmān viṣṇur āruṇiḥ 
haviṣmān anaghaś caite bhavyāḥ saptarṣayas tathā  ViP 
sarvagaḥ sarvadharmā ca devānīkādayas tathā 
bhaviṣyanti manos tasya tanayāḥ pṛthivīśvarāḥ  ViP 
rudraputras tu sāvarṇir bhavitā dvādaśo manuḥ 
ṛtadhāmā ca tatrendro bhavitā śṛṇu me surān  ViP 
haritā lohitā devās tathā sumanaso dvija 
sukarmāṇaḥ supārāś ca daśakāḥ pañca vai gaṇāḥ  ViP 
tapasvī sutapāś caiva tapomūrtis taporatiḥ 
tapodhṛtir dyutiś cānyaḥ saptamas tu tapodhanaḥ  ViP 
devavān upadevaś ca devaśreṣṭhādayas tathā 
manos tasya mahāvīryā bhaviṣyanti sutā nṛpāḥ  ViP 
trayodaśo raucyanāmā bhaviṣyati mune manuḥ  ViP 
sutrāmāṇaḥ sukarmāṇaḥ sudharmāṇas tathā surāḥ 
trayas triṃśadvibhedās te devānāṃ ye tu vai gaṇāḥ  ViP 
divaspatir mahāvīryas teṣām indro bhaviṣyati  ViP 
nirmohas tattvadarśī ca niṣprakampo nirutsukaḥ 
dhṛtimān avyayaś cānyaḥ saptamaḥ sutapā muniḥ 
saptarṣayas tv ime tasya putrān api nibodha me  ViP 
citrasenavicitrādyā bhaviṣyanti mahīkṣitaḥ  ViP

śucir indraḥ suragaṇās tatra pañca śṛṇuṣva tān  ViP

kathitā muniśārdūla pālayiṣyanti ye mahīm  ViP

pravartayanti tān etya bhuvi saptarṣayo divaḥ  ViP

tadanvayodbhavaiś caiva tāvad bhūḥ paripālyate  ViP

manvantare bhavanty ete śakraś caivādhikāriṇaḥ  ViP

sahasrayugaparyantaḥ kalpo niḥśeṣa ucyate  ViP 
tāvatpramāṇā ca niśā tato bhavati sattama

trailokyam akhilaṃ grastvā bhagavān ādikṛd vibhuḥ 
svamāyāsaṃsthito vipra sarvabhūto janārdanaḥ  ViP 
tataḥ prabuddho bhagavān yathā pūrvaṃ tathā punaḥ 
sṛṣṭiṃ karoty avyayātmā kalpe kalpe rajoguṇaḥ  ViP 
manavo bhūbhujaḥ sendrā devāḥ saptarṣayas tathā 
sāttviko 'ṃśaḥ sthitikaro jagato dvijasattama  ViP 
caturyuge 'py asau viṣṇuḥ sthitivyāpāralakṣaṇaḥ 
yugavyavasthāṃ kurute yathā maitreya tac chṛṇu  ViP 
kṛte yuge paraṃ jñānaṃ kapilādisvarūpadhṛk 
dadāti sarvabhūtātmā sarvabhūtahite rataḥ  ViP 
cakravartisvarūpeṇa tretāyām api sa prabhuḥ 
duṣṭānāṃ nigrahaṃ kurvan paripāti jagattrayam  ViP 
vedam ekaṃ caturbhedaṃ kṛtvā śākhāśatair vibhuḥ 
karoti bahulaṃ bhūyo vedavyāsasvarūpadhṛk  ViP 
vedāṃs tu dvāpare vyasya kaler ante punar hariḥ 
kalkisvarūpī durvṛttān mārge sthāpayati prabhuḥ  ViP 
evam eṣa jagat sarvaṃ paripāti karoti ca 
hanti cānteṣv anantātmā nāsty asmād vyatireki yat  ViP 
bhūtaṃ bhavyaṃ bhaviṣyaṃ ca sarvabhūtān mahātmanaḥ 
tad atrānyatra vā vipra sadbhāvaḥ kathitas tava  ViP 
manvantarāṇy aśeṣāṇi kathitāni mayā tava 
manvantarādhipāṃś caiva kim anyat kathayāmi te  ViP 
iti śrīviṣṇupurāṇe tṛtīyāṃśe dvitīyo 'dhyāyaḥ 
maitreya uvāca
jñātam etan mayā tvatto yathā sarvam idaṃ jagat 
viṣṇur viṣṇau viṣṇutaś ca na paraṃ vidyate tataḥ  ViP 
etat tu śrotum icchāmi vyastā vedā mahātmanā 
vedavyāsasvarūpeṇa yathā tena yuge yuge  ViP 
yasmin yasmin yuge vyāso yo ya āsīn mahāmune 
taṃ tam ācakṣva bhagavañ śākhābhedāṃś ca me vada  ViP 
parāśara uvāca
vedadrumasya maitreya śākhābhedaiḥ sahasraśaḥ 
na śakyo vistaro vaktuṃ saṃkṣepeṇa śṛṇuṣva tam  ViP

vedam ekaṃ sa bahudhā kurute jagato hitaḥ  ViP

vedavyāsābhidhānā tu sā mūrtir madhuvidviṣaḥ  ViP

yathā ca bhedaḥ śākhānāṃ vyāsena kriyate mune  ViP

vaivasvate 'ntare tasmin dvāpareṣu punaḥ punaḥ  ViP

dvāpare prathame vyastāḥ svayaṃ vedāḥ svayaṃbhuvā

saptame ca tathaivendro vasiṣṭhaś cāṣṭame smṛtaḥ 
sārasvataś ca navame tridhāmā daśame smṛtaḥ  ViP

somaḥ śuṣmāyaṇas tasmāt tṛṇabindur iti smṛtaḥ  ViP

aṣṭāviṃśatir ity ete vedavyāsāḥ purātanāḥ  ViP 
eko vedaś caturdhā tu yaiḥ kṛto dvāparādiṣu  ViP 
bhaviṣye dvāpare cāpi drauṇir vyāso bhaviṣyati 
vyatīte mama putre 'smin kṛṣṇadvaipāyane munau  ViP 
dhruvam ekākṣaraṃ brahma om ity evaṃ vyavasthitam 
bṛhatvād bṛṃhaṇatvāc ca tad brahmety abhidhīyate  ViP 
praṇavāvasthitaṃ nityaṃ bhūr bhuvaḥ svar itīryate 
ṛgyajuḥsāmātharvāṇaṃ yat tasmai brahmaṇe namaḥ  ViP 
jagataḥ pralayotpattau yat tat kāraṇasaṃjñitam 
mahataḥ paramaṃ guhyaṃ tasmai subrahmaṇe namaḥ  ViP

yad rūpaṃ vāsudevasya paramātmasvarūpiṇaḥ  ViP

iti śrīviṣṇupurāṇe tṛtīyāṃśe tṛtīyo 'dhyāyaḥ 
parāśara uvāca
ādyo vedaś catuṣpādaḥ śatasāhasrasaṃmitaḥ 
tato daśaguṇaḥ kṛtsno yajño 'yaṃ sarvakāmadhuk  ViP

tad anenaiva vedānāṃ śākhābhedān dvijottama 
caturyugeṣu racitān samasteṣv avadhāraya  ViP 
kṛṣṇadvaipāyanaṃ vyāsaṃ viddhi nārāyaṇaṃ prabhum

sūtaṃ jagrāha śiṣyaṃ sa itihāsapurāṇayoḥ  ViP 
ŚDG ins

DTG ins
etāni pañcanāmāni saṃhitāyāḥ samāśritāḥ  ViP

parāśara uvāca
yajurvedataroḥ śākhāḥ saptaviṃśan mahāmatiḥ

ŚD ins

parāśara uvāca
punas tayoktaṃ taj jñātvā satyaṃ satyavatāṃ varaḥ 
kānane sa nirāhāras tatyāja svaṃ kalevaram  ViP 
bhūyas tato vṛkaṃ jātaṃ gatvā taṃ nirjane vane 
smārayām āsa bhartāraṃ pūrvavṛttam aninditā  ViP 
na tvaṃ vṛko mahābhāga rājā śatadhanur bhavān 
śvā bhūtvā tvaṃ śṛgālo 'bhūr vṛkatvaṃ sāmprataṃ gataḥ  ViP 
parāśara uvāca
smāritena yathā vyaktas tenātmā gṛdhratāṃ gataḥ 
apāpā sā punaś cainaṃ bodhayām āsa bhāminī  ViP 
narendra smaryatām ātmā hy alaṃ te gṛdhraceṣṭayā 
pāṣaṇḍālāpajāto 'yaṃ doṣo yad gṛdhratāṃ gataḥ  ViP 
tataḥ kākatvam āpannaṃ samanantarajanmani 
uvāca tanvī bhartāram upalabhyātmayogataḥ  ViP 
aśeṣā bhūbhṛtaḥ pūrvaṃ vaśyā yasmai baliṃ daduḥ 
sa tvaṃ kākatvam āpanno jāto 'dya balibhuk prabho  ViP 
evam eva ca kākatve smāritaḥ sa purātanam 
tatyāja bhūpatiḥ prāṇān mayūratvam avāpa ca  ViP 
mayūratve tataḥ sā vai cakārānugataṃ śubhā 
dattaiḥ pratikṣaṇaṃ bhojyair bālā tajjātibhojanaiḥ  ViP 
tatas tu janako rājā vājimedhaṃ mahākratum 
cakāra tasyāvabhṛthe snāpayām āsa taṃ tadā  ViP 
sasnau svayaṃ ca tanvaṅgī smārayām āsa cāpi tam 
yathāsau śvaśṛgālādyā yonīr jagrāha pārthivaḥ  ViP 
smṛtajanmakramaḥ so 'tha tatyāja svaṃ kalevaram 
jajñe ca janakasyaiva putro 'sau sumahātmanaḥ  ViP 
tataḥ sā pitaraṃ tanvī vivāhārtham acodayat 
sa cāpi kārayām āsa pitā tasyāḥ svayaṃvaram  ViP 
svayaṃvare kṛte sā taṃ saṃprāptaṃ patim ātmanaḥ 
varayām āsa bhūyo 'pi bhartṛbhāvena bhāminī  ViP 
bubhuje ca tayā sārdhaṃ saṃbhogān nṛpanandanaḥ 
pitary uparate rājyaṃ videheṣu cakāra saḥ  ViP 
iyāja yajñān subahūn dadau dānāni cārthinām 
putrān utpādayām āsa yuyudhe ca sahāribhiḥ  ViP 
rājyaṃ kṛtvā yathānyāyaṃ pālayitvā vasuṃdharām 
tatyāja sa priyān prāṇān saṃgrāme dharmato nṛpaḥ  ViP 
tataś citāsthaṃ taṃ bhūyo bhartāraṃ sā śubhekṣaṇā 
anvāruroha vidhivad yathāpūrvaṃ mudāvatī  ViP 
tato 'vāpa tayā sārdhaṃ rājaputryā sa pārthivaḥ 
aindrān atītya vai lokāṃl lokān kāmaduho 'kṣayān  ViP 
svargākṣayatvam atulaṃ dāmpatyam atidurlabham 
prāptaṃ puṇyaphalaṃ prāpya saṃśuddhiṃ tāṃ dvijottama  ViP 
eṣa pāṣaṇḍasaṃbhāṣadoṣaḥ prokto mayā dvija 
tathāśvamedhāvabhṛthasnānamāhātmyam eva ca  ViP 
tasmāt pāṣaṇḍibhiḥ pāpair ālāpasparśanaṃ tyajet 
viśeṣataḥ kriyākāle yajñādau cāpi dīkṣitaḥ  ViP 
kriyāhānir gṛhe yasya māsam ekaṃ prajāyate 
tasyāvalokanāt sūryaṃ paśyeta matimān naraḥ  ViP 
kiṃ punar yais tu saṃtyaktā trayī sarvātmanā dvija 
parānnabhojibhiḥ pāpair vedavādavirodhibhiḥ  ViP

brahmovāca
na hy ādimadhyāntam ajasya yasya vidmo vayaṃ sarvamayasya dhātuḥ

tasya ca samastā eva putrā dhundhumukhaniḥśvāsāgninā vipluṣṭā vineśuḥ  ViP 
dṛḍhāśvacandrāśvakapilāśvās trayaḥ kevalaṃ avaśeṣitāḥ  ViP 
dṛḍhāśvād dharyaśvas tasmān nikumbho nikumbhāt saṃhitāśvaḥ 
tataś ca kṛśāśvas

tasyāṃ ca madhyarātrinivṛttāyāṃ mantrapūtajalapūrṇaṃ kalaśaṃ vedimadhye niveśya te munayaḥ suṣupuḥ  ViP

suptāṃś ca tān ṛṣīn naivotthāpayām āsa 
tac ca kalaśajalam aparimeyamāhātmyaṃ mantrapūtaṃ papau  ViP 
prabuddhāś ca ṛṣayaḥ papracchuḥ kenaitan mantrapūtaṃ vāri pītam  ViP 
atra hi pīte rājño yuvanāśvasya patnī mahābalaparākramaṃ putraṃ janayiṣyatīty ākarṇya sa rājā ajānatā mayā pītam ity āha  ViP

prāptasamayaś ca dakṣiṇakukṣim avanīpater nirbhidya niścakrāma na cāsau rājā mamāra  ViP 
jāto nāmaiṣa kaṃ dhāsyatīti munayaḥ procuḥ  ViP 
athāgamya devarāḍ abravīt mām ayaṃ dhāsyatīti  ViP 
tato māṃdhātā nāmato 'bhavat

tāṃ cāmṛtasrāviṇīm āsvādyāhnaiva sa vyavardhata  ViP 
sa tu māṃdhātā cakravartī saptadvīpāṃ mahīṃ bubhuje  ViP 
bhavati cātra ślokaḥ 
yāvat sūrya udeti sma yāvac ca pratitiṣṭhati

māṃdhātā śaśabindor duhitaraṃ bindumatīm upayeme 
purukutsam ambarīṣaṃ ca mucakundaṃ ca tasyāṃ putratrayam utpādayām āsa  ViP 
pañcāśac ca duhitaras tasya nṛpater babhūvuḥ  ViP 
bahvṛcaś ca saubharir nāma ṛṣir antarjale dvādaśābdaṃ kālam uvāsa  ViP 
tatra cāntarjale saṃmado nāmātibahuprajo 'tipramāṇo mīnādhipatir āsīt 
 tasya ca putrapautradauhitrāḥ pārśvataḥ pṛṣṭhato 'grato vakṣaḥpucchaśirasāṃ copari bhramantas tenaiva sahāharniśam atinirvṛtā remire  ViP 
 sa cāpi tatsparśopacīyamānaharṣaprakarṣo bahuprakāraṃ tasya ṛṣeḥ paśyatas tair ātmajapautradauhitrādibhiḥ sahānudinaṃ bahuprakāraṃ reme  
 athāntarjalāvasthitaḥ sa saubharir ekāgratāsamādhānam apahāyānudinaṃ tat tasya matsyasyātmajapautradauhitrādibhiḥ sahātiramaṇīyaṃ lalitam avekṣyācintayat 
aho dhanyo 'yam īdṛśam apy anabhimataṃ yonyantaram avāpyaibhir ātmajapautrādibhiḥ saha ramamāṇo 'tīvāsmākaṃ spṛhām utpādayati 
vayam apy evaṃ putrādibhiḥ saha ramiṣyāmaḥ 
ity evam abhisamīkṣya sa tasmād antarjalān niṣkramya nirveṣṭukāmaḥ kanyārthaṃ māṃdhātāraṃ rājānam agacchat  ViP 
āgamanaśravaṇasamanantaraṃ cotthāya tena rājñā samyag arghādinā pūjitaḥ kṛtāsanaparigrahaḥ saubharir uvāca  ViP 
saubharir uvāca
nirveṣṭukāmo 'smi narendra kanyāṃ prayaccha me mā praṇayaṃ vibhāṅkṣīḥ 
na hy arthinaḥ kāryavaśābhyupetāḥ kakutsthagotre vimukhāḥ prayānti  ViP

parāśara uvāca
 iti ṛṣivacanam ākarṇya sa rājā jarājarjaritadehaṃ tam ṛṣim ālokya pratyākhyānakātaras tasmāc ca bhagavataḥ śāpato bibhyatkiṃcidadhomukhaś ciraṃ

rājovāca

katham apy eṣā saṃjātā tad evam upasthite na vidmaḥ kiṃ kurma ity etan mayā cintyate 
ity abhihite ca tena bhūbhujā munir acintayat 
aho 'yam anyo 'smatpratyākhyānopāyo vṛddho 'yam anabhimataḥ strīṇāṃ kim uta kanyānām ity amunā saṃcintyaivam abhihitam 
evam astu tathā kariṣyāmīti saṃcintya māṃdhātāram uvāca  ViP 
yady evaṃ tadādiśyatām asmākaṃ praveśāya kanyāntaḥpuravarṣavaraḥ 
yadi kanyaiva kācin mām abhilaṣati tadāhaṃ dārasaṃgrahaṃ kariṣyāmīty anyathā cet tad alam asmākam etenātītakālārambhenety uktvā virarāma 
parāśara uvāca
tataś ca māṃdhātrā muniśāpaśaṅkitena kanyāntaḥpuravarṣavaraḥ samājñaptaḥ  ViP 
kanyāntaḥpuraṃ praviśann eva bhagavān akhilasiddhagandharvamanuṣyebhyo 'tiśayena kamanīyaṃ rūpam akarot  ViP 
praveśya ca tam ṛṣim antaḥpuravarṣavaras tāḥ kanyakāḥ prāha  ViP 
bhavatīnāṃ janayitā mahārājaḥ samājñāpayati 
ayam asmān brahmarṣiḥ kanyārthī samabhyāgato mayā cāsya pratijñātaṃ yady asmatkanyakā
kācid bhagavantaṃ varayati tat kanyāyāś chande nāhaṃ paripanthānaṃ kariṣyāmīty ākarṇya
sarvā eva tāḥ kanyāḥ sānurāgāḥ samanmathāḥ kareṇava ivebhayūthapatiṃ tam ṛṣim ahamahamikayā

ūcuś ca
alaṃ bhaginyo 'ham imaṃ vṛṇomi vṛto mayā naiṣa tavānurūpaḥ

vṛto mayāyaṃ prathamaṃ mayāyaṃ gṛhaṃ viśann eva vihanyase kim

tadā sa kanyādhikṛto nṛpāya yathāvad ācaṣṭa vinamramūrtiḥ  ViP 
parāśara uvāca
tadavagamāt kiṃ kim etat kathaya kiṃ karomīti kiṃ mayābhihitam ity ākulamatir anicchann api kathamapi rājānumene  ViP

tatra cāśeṣaśilpiśilpapraṇetāraṃ dhātāram ivānyaṃ viśvakarmāṇam āhūya sakalakanyānām

tac ca tathaivānuṣṭhitam aśeṣaśilpaviśeṣācāryas tvaṣṭā darśitavān  ViP

tato 'navaratabhakṣyabhojyalehyādyupabhogair āgatānugatabhṛtyādīn aharniśam aśeṣagṛheṣu tāḥ kṣitīśaduhitaro bhojayām āsuḥ  ViP

praviśya caikaṃ prāsādam ātmajāṃ pariṣvajya kṛtāsanaparigrahaḥ pravṛddhasnehanayanāmbugarbhanayano 'bravīt  ViP

aho me mohasyātivistāraḥ  ViP 
manorathānāṃ na samāptir asti varṣāyutenāpi tathābdalakṣaiḥ

cīrṇaṃ tapo yat tu jalāśrayeṇa tasyarddhir eṣā tapaso 'ntarāyaḥ

ahaṃ cariṣyāmi tathātmano 'rthe parigrahagrāhagṛhītabuddhiḥ

 ity ātmānam ātmanaivābhidhāyāsau saubharir apahāya putragṛhāsanaparicchadādikam aśeṣam arthajātaṃ sakalabhāryāsamaveto vanaṃ praviveśa  ViP

praṇipatyābhihitaḥ  
bhagavann apy asmākam etebhyo gandharvebhyo bhayam upaśamam eṣyatīti āha bhagavān
anādipuruṣaḥ puruṣottamo yauvanāśvasya māṃdhātuḥ purukutsanāmā putras tam aham anupraviśya

atra ca ślokaḥ 
narmadāyai namaḥ prātar narmadāyai namo niśi

ity uccāryāharniśam andhakārapraveśe vā na sarpair daśyate na cāpi kṛtānusmaraṇabhujo viṣam api bhuktam upaghātāya bhaviṣyati  ViP

 dvādaśavārṣikyām anāvṛṣṭyāṃ viśvāmitrakalatrāpatyapoṣaṇārthaṃ cāṇḍālapratigrahapariharaṇāya jāhnavītīranyagrodhe mṛgamāṃsam anudinaṃ babandha

tasyāś ca sapatnyā garbhastambhanāya garo dattaḥ  ViP 
tenāsyā garbhaḥ saptavarṣāṇi jaṭhara eva tasthau

maivaṃ maivaṃ sāhasādhyavasāyinī bhavetyukte ca sā tasmād anumaraṇanirbandhād virarāma  ViP

kṛtopanayanaṃ cainam aurvo vedaśāstrāṇy astraṃ cāgneyaṃ bhārgavākhyam adhyāpayām āsa  ViP

sa tatheti tad guruvacanam abhinandya teṣāṃ veṣānyatvam akārayat yavanān muṇḍitaśiraso

prasāditaḥ

maitreya uvāca

 tataḥ sphuraducchvasitāmalakapolakāntir bhagavān uḍupatis tam āliṅgya kumāraṃ sādhu sādhu vatsa prājño 'sīti budha iti nāma cakre  ViP

rajeḥ pañca putraśatāny atulavīryasārāṇy āsan  ViP

tatputraḥ saṃjayas tasyāpi jayas tataś ca vijayas tasmāc ca jajñe kṛtaḥ 
tasya harṣavardhano harṣavardhanasutaḥ sahadevas tasmād adīnas tasya jayatsenaḥ tataś
ca saṃkṛtis tatputraḥ kṣatradharmā ity ete kṣatravṛddhasyāto nahuṣavaṃśaṃ pravakṣyāmīti  ViP 
iti śrīviṣṇupurāṇe caturthe 'ṃśe navamo 'dhyāyaḥ 
parāśara uvāca
yatiyayātisaṃyātyāyātiviyātikṛtisaṃjñā nahuṣasya ṣaṭ putrā mahābalaparākramā babhūvuḥ  ViP 
yatis tu rājyaṃ naicchat 
yayātis tu bhūbhṛd abhavat  ViP 
uśanasaś ca duhitaraṃ devayānīṃ śarmiṣṭhāṃ ca vārṣaparvaṇīm upayeme 
atrānuvaṃśaśloko bhavati  ViP 
yaduṃ ca turvasuṃ caiva devayānī vyajāyata 
druhyuṃ cānuṃ ca pūruṃ ca śarmiṣṭhā vārṣaparvaṇī  ViP 
kāvyaśāpāc cākālenaiva yayātir jarām avāpa  ViP 
prasannaśukravacanāc ca svajarāṃ saṃkrāmayituṃ jyeṣṭhaputraṃ yadum uvāca  ViP 
tvanmātāmahaśāpād iyam akālenaiva jarā mām upasthitā 
tām ahaṃ tasyaivānugrahād bhavataḥ saṃcārayāmy ekaṃ varṣasahasram atṛpto 'smi viṣayeṣu tvadvayasā viṣayān ahaṃ bhoktum icchāmi 
nātra bhavatā pratyākhyānaṃ kartavyam ity uktaḥ sa naicchat tāṃ jarām ādātum 
taṃ cāpi pitā śaśāpa 
tvatprasūtir na rājyārhā bhaviṣyatīti  ViP 
anantaraṃ ca durvasuṃ druhyum anuṃ ca pṛthivīpatir jarāgrahaṇārthaṃ svayauvanapradānāya cābhyarthayām āsa 
tair apy ekaikaśyena pratyākhyātas tāñ chaśāpa  ViP 
atha śarmiṣṭhātanayam aśeṣakanīyāṃsaṃ pūruṃ tathaivāha 
sa cātipravaṇamatiḥ praṇamya pitaraṃ sabahumānaṃ mahān prasādo 'yam asmākam ity udāram abhidhāya jarāṃ pratijagrāha 
svakīyaṃ ca yauvanaṃ pitre dadau  ViP 
so 'pi pauravaṃ yauvanam āsādya dharmāvirodhena yathākāmaṃ yathākālopapannaṃ yathotsāhaṃ viṣayāṃś cacāra 
samyak ca prajāpālanam akarot  ViPḥ
viśvācyā devayānyā ca sahopabhogaṃ bhuktvā kāmānām antam avāpsyāmīty anudinaṃ tanmanasko babhūva  ViP 
anudinaṃ copabhogataḥ kāmān atīvābhiramyān mene  ViP 
tataś caivam agāyata 
na jātu kāmaḥ kāmānām upabhogena śāmyati 
haviṣā kṛṣṇavartmeva bhūya evābhivardhate  ViP 
yat pṛthivyāṃ vrīhiyavaṃ hiraṇyaṃ paśavaḥ striyaḥ 
ekasyāpi na paryāptaṃ tasmāt tṛṣṇāṃ parityajet  ViP 
yadā na kurute bhāvaṃ sarvabhūteṣu pāpakam 
samadṛṣṭes tadā puṃsaḥ sarvāḥ sukhamayā diśaḥ  ViP 
yā dustyajā durmatibhir yā na jīryati jīryataḥ 
tāṃ tṛṣṇāṃ saṃtyajet prājñaḥ sukhenaivābhipūryate  ViP 
jīryanti jīryataḥ keśā dantā jīryanti jīryataḥ 
dhanāśā jīvitāśā ca jīryato 'pi na jīryataḥ  ViP 
pūrṇaṃ varṣasahasraṃ me viṣayāsaktacetasaḥ 
tathāpy anudinaṃ tṛṣṇā mamaiteṣv eva jāyate  ViP 
tasmād etām ahaṃ tyaktvā brahmaṇy ādhāya mānasam 
nirdvandvo nirmamo bhūtvā cariṣyāmi mṛgaiḥ saha  ViP 
parāśara uvāca
pūroḥ sakāśād ādāya jarāṃ dattvā ca yauvanam 
rājye 'bhiṣicya pūruṃ ca prayayau tapase vanam  ViP 
diśi dakṣiṇapūrvāyāṃ turvasuṃ praty athādiśat 
pratīcyāṃ ca tathā druhyuṃ dakṣiṇāyāṃ tato yadum  ViP 
udīcyāṃ ca tathaivānuṃ kṛtvā maṇḍalino nṛpān 
sarvapṛthvīpatiṃ pūruṃ so 'bhiṣicya yayau vanam  ViP 
iti śrīviṣṇupurāṇe caturthe 'ṃśe daśamo 'dhyāyaḥ 
parāśara uvāca
ataḥ paraṃ yayāteḥ prathamaputrasya yador vaṃśam ahaṃ kathayāmi 
yatrāśeṣalokanivāsimanuṣyasiddhagandharvayakṣarākṣasaguhyakakiṃpuruṣāpsaroragavihagadaityadānavarudravasvaśvi

kṛtavīryād arjunaḥ saptadvīpapatir bāhusahasrī jajñe

daśa yajñasahasrāṇy asāv ayajat  ViP 
tasya ca śloko 'dyāpi gīyate 
na nūnaṃ kārtavīryasya gatiṃ yāsyanti pārthivāḥ 
yajñair dānais tapobhir vā praśrayeṇa śrutena ca  ViP 
anaṣṭadravyatā ca tasya rājye 'bhavat

tasya ca putraśatapradhānāḥ pañca putrā babhūvuḥ

parāśara uvāca
kroṣṭoś ca yaduputrasyātmajo vṛjinīvān

ruṣaṅkoś citrarathaḥ 
tattanayaḥ śaśabinduś caturdaśamahāratnaś cakravarty abhavat

parāśara uvāca
ity ātmerṣyākopakaluṣitavacanamuṣitavivekatayā duruktaparihārārtham idam avanīpatir āha 
 yas te janiṣyaty ātmajas tasyeyam anāgata eva bhāryā nirūpitety ākarṇyodbhūtamṛduhāsā tathety āha praviveśa ca rājñā sahādhiṣṭhānam  ViP 
 anantaraṃ cātiśuddhalagnahorāṃśakāvayavoktakṛtaputrajanmālāpaguṇād vayasaḥ pariṇāmam upagatāpi śaibyā svalpair evāhobhir garbham avāpa  ViP

bhajanabhajamānadivyāndhakadevāvṛdhamahābhojavṛṣṇi saṃjñāḥ satvatasya putrā babhūvuḥ  ViP

dvārakāvāsijanapadas tu tam āyāntam avekṣya bhagavantam ādipuruṣaṃ puruṣottamam avanibhārāvataraṇāyāṃśena mānuṣarūpadhāriṇaṃ praṇipatyāha

anyathā ya enaṃ dhārayati tam eva hantīty 
asāv api prasenaḥ syamantakena kaṇṭhāsaktenāśvam āruhyāṭavyāṃ mṛgayām agacchat 
tatra ca siṃhād vadham avāpa 
sāśvaṃ ca taṃ nihatya siṃho 'py amalamaṇiratnam āsyāgreṇādāya gantum udyata ṛkṣādhipatinā jāmbavatā dṛṣṭo ghātitaś ca 
jāmbavān apy amalaṃ tan maṇiratnam ādāya svabilaṃ praviveśa 
sukumārasaṃjñāya ca bālakāya krīḍanakam akarot  ViP 
anāgacchati ca tasmin prasene kṛṣṇo maṇiratnam abhilaṣitavān 
na ca prāptavān nūnam etad asya karmety akhila eva yadulokaḥ parasparaṃ karṇākarṇy'kathayat  ViP 
viditalokāpavādavṛttāntaś ca bhagavān yadusainyaparivāraḥ prasenāśvapadavīm anusasāra 
dadarśa cāśvasametaṃ prasenaṃ nihataṃ siṃhenākhilajanapadamadhye siṃhapadadarśanakṛtapariśuddhiḥ siṃhapadam anusasāra  ViP 
ṛkṣavinihataṃ ca siṃham apy alpe bhūmibhāge dṛṣṭvā tataś ca tadratnagauravād ṛkṣasyāpi padāny anuyayau 
giritaṭe ca sakalam eva yadusainyam avasthāpya tatpadānusārī ṛkṣabilaṃ praviveśa 
ardhapraviṣṭaś ca dhātryāḥ sukumārakam ullāpayantyā vāṇīṃ śuśrāva 
siṃhaḥ prasenam avadhīt siṃho jāmbavatā hataḥ 
sukumāraka mā rodīs tava hy eṣa syamantakaḥ  ViP 
ity ākarṇyalabdhasyamantakodantaḥ praviṣṭaḥ kumārakrīḍanakīkṛtaṃ ca dhātryā haste tejobhir jājvalyamānaṃ syamantakaṃ dadarśa  ViP
taṃ ca syamantakābhilāṣicakṣuṣam apūrvapuruṣam āgataṃ samavekṣya dhātrī trāhi trāhīti vyājahāra  ViP 
tadārtanādaśravaṇānantaraṃ cāmarṣapūrṇahṛdayaḥ sa jāmbavān ājagāma 
tayoś ca parasparam yudhyator dvayor yuddham ekaviṃśatidināny abhavat 
te ca yadusainikās tatra saptāṣṭa dināni tanniṣkrāntim udīkṣamāṇās tasthuḥ 
aniṣkramamāṇe ca madhuripāv asāv avaśyam atra bile 'tyantaṃ nāśam āpto bhaviṣyaty
anyathā tasya jīvataḥ katham etāvanti dināni śatrujaye vyākṣepo bhavatīti kṛtādhyavasāyā
dvārakām āgatya hataḥ kṛṣṇa iti kathayām āsuḥ  ViP 
tadbāndhavāś ca tatkālocitam akhilam uparatakriyākalāpaṃ cakruḥ 
tatrāsya yuddhyamānasyātiśraddhādattaviśiṣṭapātropayuktānnatoyādinā kṛṣṇasya balaprāṇapuṣṭir abhūt  ViP 
itarasyānudinam atigurupuruṣabhidyamānasyātiniṣṭhuraprahārapīḍitākhilāvayavasya nirāhāratayā balahāniḥ 
nirjitaś ca bhagavatā jāmbavān praṇipatyāha V vyājahāra 
asurasurayakṣagandharvarākṣasādibhir apy akhilair bhagavān na jetuṃ śakyaḥ 
kim utāvanigocarair alpavīryair narair narāvayavabhūtaiś ca tiryagyonyanusṛtibhiḥ kiṃ punar asmadvidhaiḥ 
 avaśyaṃ bhagavato 'smatsvāmino nārāyaṇasya sakalajagatparāyaṇasyāṃśena bhagavatā bhavitavyam ity uktas tasmai bhagavān akhilāvanibhārāvatāram  
ācacakṣe  
prītyābhyañjitakaratalasparśanena cainam apagatayuddhakhedaṃ cakāra  ViP 
sa ca praṇipatyainaṃ punar api prasādya jāmbavatīṃ nāma kanyāṃ gṛhāgamanārghyabhūtāṃ grāhayām āsa  ViP 
syamantakamaṇim apy asau praṇipatya tasmai pradadau 
acyuto 'py atipraṇatāt tasmād agrāhyam api tan maṇiratnam ātmasaṃśodhanāya jagrāha  ViP

tāṃ cākrūrakṛtavarmaśatadhanvapramukhā yādavāḥ pūrvaṃ varayāṃ āsuḥ 
tatas tatpradānād avajñātam ivātmānaṃ manyamānāḥ satrājite vairānubandhaṃ cakruḥ  ViP 
akrūrakṛtavarmapramukhāś ca śatadhanvānam ūcuḥ

gate ca tasmin suptam eva satrājitaṃ śatadhanvā jaghāna maṇiratnaṃ cādade

nāham etāṃ tasya durātmanaḥ sahiṣye 
na hy anullaṅghya varapādapaṃ tatkṛtanīḍāśrayiṇo vihaṃgā vadhyante 
tad alam atyartham amunāsmatpurataḥ śokapreritavākyaparikareṇety uktvā dvārakām abhyetya baladevam ekānte vāsudevaḥ prāha

tadubhayavināśāt tan maṇiratnam āvābhyāṃ sāmānyaṃ bhaviṣyati  ViP

kṛtodyogau ca tāv ubhāv upalabhya śatadhanvā kṛtavarmāṇam upetya pārṣṇipūraṇakarmanimittam acodayat 
āha cainaṃ kṛtavarmā 
nāhaṃ balabhadravāsudevābhyāṃ saha virodhāyālam ity uktaś cākrūram acodayat

vṛthaivāsmābhir ghātitaḥ śatadhanvā

dhik tvāṃ yas tvam evam arthalipsur etac ca te bhrātṛtvān marṣaye

 putri kasmān na jāyase niṣkramyatām āsyaṃ te draṣṭum icchāmy ahaṃ svakāṃ ca mātaraṃ kim iti ciraṃ kleśayiṣyasīty ukte garbhasthaiva vyājahāra

ānītaḥ  
tatra cāgatamātra eva tasya tatsthasya maṇer anubhāvad anāvṛṣṭimarakadurbhikṣavyālādyupadravaḥ śaśāma

sumahāṃś cāyam anāvṛṣṭidurbhikṣamarakādyupadravaśamanakārī prabhāvaḥ  ViP

 alpopādānaṃ cāsyā saṃśayam atrāsau varamaṇis tiṣṭhatīti kṛtādhyavasāyo 'nyat prayojanam uddiśya sakalayādavasamājam ātmageha evācīkarat  
 tatra copaviṣṭeṣv akhileṣu yādaveṣu pūrvaprayojanam upanyasya paryavasite ca tasmin prasaṅgāgataparihāsakathām akrūreṇa saha kṛtvā janārdanas

 dānapate jānīma eva vayaṃ yathā śatadhanvanā tad akhilajagatsārabhūtaṃ syamantakaratnaṃ bhavataḥ samarpitaṃ tad etad rāṣṭropakārakaṃ bhavataḥ  
sakāśe tiṣṭhatīti  
 tiṣṭhatu sarva eva vayaṃ tatprabhāvaphalabhujaḥ kiṃ tv eṣa balabhadro 'smān āśaṅkitavāṃs tad asmatprītaye darśayety abhihitaḥ saratnaḥ so 'cintayat 
kim atrānuṣṭheyam anyathā ced bravīmy ahaṃ tat kevalāmbaratirodhānam anviṣyanto ratnam
etad drakṣyantīty anveṣaṇaṃ na kṣemam iti saṃcintya tam akhilajagatkāraṇabhūtaṃ nārāyaṇam āhākrūraḥ 
bhagavan mamaitat syamantakaratnaṃ śatadhanvanā samarpitam  ViP 
apagate ca tasminn adya śvaḥ paraśvo vā bhagavān māṃ yācayiṣyatīti etāvantaṃ kālam atikṛcchreṇādhārayam

etāvanmātram apy aśeṣarāṣṭropakārī dhārayituṃ na śaknotīti māṃ bhavān maṃsyata ity ātmanā na coditam  ViP

tataḥ so 'dharavastranigopitātilaghukanakasamudgakaṃ pragaṭīkṛtavān  ViP

athāhākrūraḥ 
sa eṣa maṇir yaḥ śatadhanvanāsmākaṃ samarpito yasyāyaṃ sa enaṃ gṛhṇātv iti

mamedaṃ pitṛdhanam ity atīva ca satyabhāmā spṛhāṃ cakāra

 etad dhi maṇiratnam ātmasaṃśodhanāya eṣāṃ yadūnāṃ darśitam etac ca mama balabhadrasya ca sāmānyaṃ pitṛdhanaṃ caitat satyabhāmāyā nānyasya  
etat sarvakālaṃ śucinā brahmacaryeṇa dhriyamāṇam aśeṣarāṣṭrasyopakārakam aśucinā dhriyamāṇam ādhāram eva hanti  ViP 
ato 'ham asya ṣoḍaśastrīsahasraparigrahād asamartho dhāraṇe 
katham caitat satyabhāmā svīkarotu 
āryabalabhadreṇāpi madirāpānādyaśeṣopabhogaparityāgaḥ kathaṃ kāryaḥ 
tad ayaṃ yaduloko 'haṃ balabhadraḥ satyā ca tvāṃ dānapate prārthayāmaḥ 
etad bhavān eva dhārayituṃ samarthaḥ 
tvadsthaṃ cāsya rāṣṭrasyopakārakaṃ tad bhavān aśeṣarāṣṭropakāranimittam etat pūrvavad dhārayatu 
tvayānyan na vaktavyam ity ukto dānapatis tathety uktvā jagrāha ca tan mahāratnam 
tataḥ prabhṛti ca akrūraḥ prakaṭenaivātitejasā jājjvalyamānenātmakaṇṭhāsaktenāditya ivāṃśumālī cacāra  ViP 
ity etāṃ bhagavato mithyābhiśastikṣālanāṃ yaḥ smarati na tasya kadācid alpāpi mithyābhiśastir bhavati 
avyāhatendriyaś cākhilapāpamokṣam avāpnotīti  ViP 
iti śrīviṣṇupurāṇe caturthe 'ṃśe trayodaśo 'dhyāyaḥ 
parāśara uvāca
anamitrasya sutaḥ śinir nāmābhavat 
tasyāpi satyakaḥ satyakāt sātyakir yuyudhānanāmā 
tasmād apy asaṅgas tatputraś ca tūṇis tūṇer yugaṃdharaḥ 
iti śaineyāḥ  ViP 
anamitrasyaivānvaye vṛṣṇiḥ 
tasmāc ca śvaphalkas tatprabhāvaḥ kathita eva 
śvaphalkasya kanīyāṃś citrako nāmābhavad bhrātā 
śvaphalkād akrūro gāndinyām abhavat 
 tathopamadgur upamadgor mṛduraviśārimejayagirikṣatropakṣatraśatrughnārimardanadharmadṛgdṛṣṭavarmagandhamojavāhaprativāhākhyāḥ putrāḥ sutārākhyā  
ca kanyā  
devavān upadevaś cākrūraputrau 
pṛthuvipṛthupramukhāś citrakasya putrā bahavo 'bhavan
kukurabhajamānaśucikambalabarhiṣākhyās tathāndhakasya catvāraḥ putrāḥ  ViP 
kukurād dhṛṣṭas tasmāc ca kapotaromā tataś ca vilomā 
tasmād api tumburusakhā bhavasaṃjñaś candanodakadundubhiḥ 
tataś cābhijit tataḥ punarvasuḥ 
tasyāpy āhukaḥ putra āhukī ca kanyā  ViP 
āhukasya devakograsenau dvau putrau 
devavān upadevaḥ sahadevo devarakṣito devakasyāpi catvāraḥ putrāḥ 
teṣāṃ ca vṛkadevopadevā devarakṣitā śrīdevā śāntidevā sahadevā devakī ca sapta bhaginyaḥ 
tāś ca sarvā eva vasudeva upayeme 
ugrasenasyāpi kaṃsanyagrodhasunāmakaṅkaśaṅkusubhūmirāṣṭrapālayuddhamuṣṭituṣṭimatsaṃjñāḥ putrāḥ 
kaṃsā kaṃsavatī sutanū rāṣṭrapālī kaṅkī ca ugrasenatanūjāḥ 
bhajamānāc ca vidūrathaḥ putro 'bhavat 
vidūrathāc chūraḥ śūrāc chamī śaminaḥ pratikṣatraḥ 
tasmāt svayaṃbhojas tataś ca hṛdikaḥ  ViP 
tasyāpi kṛtavarmaśatadhanurdevamīḍhuṣākhyāḥ putrā babhūvuḥ  ViP 
devamīḍhuṣasya śūrasya māriṣā nāma patny abhavat  ViP 
tasyāṃ cāsau daśa putrān ajanayad vasudevapūrvān

tatas tadaivānakadundubhisaṃjñām avāpa 
tasyāpi devabhāgadevaśravānādhṛṣṭikarundhakavatsabālakasṛñjayaśyāmaśamīkagaṇḍūṣasaṃjñā nava bhrātaro babhūvuḥ 
pṛthā śrutadevā śrutakīrtiḥ śrutaśravā rājādhidevī ca vasudevādīnāṃ pañca bhaginyo 'bhavan  ViP 
śūrasya kuntir nāma sakhābhavat 
tasmai cāputrāya pṛthām ātmajāṃ vidhinā śūro dattavān 
tāṃ ca pāṇḍur uvāha 
tasyāṃ ca dharmānilaśakrair yudhiṣṭhirabhīmārjunākhyās trayaḥ putrāḥ samutpāditāḥ 
pūrvam anūḍhāyāś ca bhagavatā bhāsvatā kānīnaḥ karṇo nāma putro 'janyata  ViP 
tasyāś ca sapatnī mādrī nāmābhavat 
nāsatyadasrābhyāṃ tasyām api nakulasahadevau pāṇḍoḥ putrau janitau 
śrutadevāṃ tu vṛddhaśarmā nāma kārūśa upayeme 
tasyāṃ dantavakro nāma mahāsuro jajñe 
śrutakīrtim api kaikeyarāja upayeme 
tasyāṃ saṃtardanādayaḥ kaikeyāḥ pañca putrā babhūvuḥ 
rājādhidevyām āvantyau vindānuvindau jajñāte 
śrutaśravasam api cedirājo damaghoṣanāmopayeme 
tasyāṃ śiśupālam utpādayām āsa 
sa hi pūrvam apy anācāravikramasaṃpanno daityānām ādipuruṣo hiraṇyakaśipur abhūt  ViP 
yaś ca bhagavatā sakalalokaguruṇā ghātitaḥ 
punar apy akṣatavīryaśauryasaṃpatparākramaguṇaḥ samākrāntasakalatrailokyeśvarapratāpo daśānano 'bhavat  ViP 
bahukālopabhuktabhagavatsakāśād avāptaśarīrapātodbhavapuṇyaphalo 'tha bhagavatāeva rāghavarūpiṇā so 'pi nidhanam upapāditaḥ 
cedirājadamaghoṣātmajaś cedipatiḥ śiśupālanāmābhavat  ViP 
śiśupālatve 'pi bhagavato bhūbhārāvatāraṇāyāvatīrṇāṃśasya puṇḍarīkanayanākhyasyopari dveṣānubandham atitarāñ cakāra 
bhagavatā ca nidhanam upanītas tatraiva paramātmabhūte manasas tadekāgratayā tatraiva sāyujyam avāpa  ViP 
bhagavān hi prasanno yathābhilaṣitaṃ dadāty aprasanno 'pi nighnan divyam anupamaṃ sthānaṃ prayacchatīti  ViP 
iti śrīviṣṇupurāṇe caturthe 'ṃśe caturdaśo 'dhyāyaḥ 
maitreya uvāca
hiraṇyakaśiputve ca rāvaṇatve ca viṣṇunā 
avāpa nihato bhogān aprāpyān amarair api  ViP 
na layaṃ tatra tenaiva nihataḥ sa kathaṃ punaḥ 
saṃprāptaḥ śiśupālatve sāyujyaṃ śāśvate harau  ViP 
etad icchāmy ahaṃ śrotuṃ sarvadharmabhṛtāṃ vara 
kautūhalapareṇaitat pṛṣṭo me vaktum arhasi  ViP 
parāśara uvāca
daityeśvarasya tu vadhāyākhilalokotpattisthitivināśakāriṇāpūrvaṃ tanugrahaṇaṃ kurvatā nṛsiṃharūpam āviṣkṛtam

putrāḥ samutpāditāḥ  
teṣāṃ ca draupadyāṃ pañca putrā babhūvuḥ 
yudhiṣṭhirāt prativindhyo bhīmasenāc chrutasomaḥ śrutakīrtir arjunāc chatānīko nakulāc chrutakarmā sahadevāt 
apare ca pāṇḍavānām ātmajās tad yathā 
yaudheyī yudhiṣṭhirād devakaṃ putram avāpa 
hiḍimbā ghaṭotkacaṃ bhīmasenāt putraṃ lebhe 
kāśī ca bhīmasenād eva sarvatragaṃ putram avāpa 
sahadevāc ca vijayā suhotraṃ nāma putraṃ prāptavatī

iti śrīviṣṇupurāṇe caturthe 'ṃśe viṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ 
parāśara uvāca
ataḥ paraṃ bhaviṣyān ahaṃ bhūpālān kīrtayiṣyāmi

 yo 'sau yājñavalkyād vedam adhītya kṛpād astrāṇy avāpya viṣayaviraktacittavṛttiś ca śaunakopadeśād ātmavijñānapravīṇaḥ paraṃ nirvāṇam āpsyati

tato npaṃjayas tato mṛdus tasmāt tigmas tigmād bṛhadrathaḥ

atrāyaṃ ślokaḥ

kṣemakaṃ prāpya rājānaṃ sa saṃsthāṃ prāpsyate kalau  ViP

ataś cekṣvākavo bhaviṣyāḥ pārthivāḥ kathyante 
bṛhadbalasya putro bṛhatkṣaṇaḥ  ViP 
tasmād urukṣayas tato vatso vatsād vatsavyūhaḥ 
tataḥ prativyomas tasyāpi divākaras tasmāt sahadevaḥ  ViP

sahasraśo 'bhyadhāvanta taṃ janaṃ nihateśvaram  ViP 
tato nivṛtya kaunteyaḥ prāhābhīrān hasann iva 
nivartadhvam adharmajñā yadi na stha mumūrṣavaḥ  ViP 
avajñāya vacas tasya jagṛhus te tadā dhanam 
strījanaṃ caiva maitreya viṣvaksenaparigraham  ViP 
tato 'rjuno dhanur divyaṃ gāṇḍīvam ajaraṃ yudhi 
āropayitum ārebhe na śaśāka ca vīryavān  ViP 
cakāra sajjaṃ kṛcchrāc ca tac cābhūc chithilaṃ punaḥ 
na sasmāra tathāstrāṇi cintayann api pāṇḍavaḥ  ViP 
śarān mumoca caiteṣu pārtho vairiṣv amarṣitaḥ 
tvagbhedaṃ te paraṃ cakrur astā gāṇḍīvadhanvanā  ViP 
vahninā ye 'kṣayā dattāḥ śarās te 'pi kṣayaṃ yayuḥ 
yudhyataḥ saha gopālair arjunasya bhavakṣaye  ViP 
acintayac ca kaunteyaḥ kṛṣṇasyaiva hi tad balam 
yan mayā śarasaṃghātaiḥ sakalā bhūbhṛto jitāḥ  ViP 
miṣataḥ pāṇḍuputrasya tatas tāḥ pramadottamāḥ 
ābhīrair apakṛṣyanta kāmāc cānyāḥ pravavrajuḥ  ViP 
tataḥ śareṣu kṣīṇeṣu dhanuṣkoṭyā dhanaṃjayaḥ 
jaghāna dasyūṃs te cāsya prahārāñ jahasur mune  ViP 
prekṣataś caiva pārthasya vṛṣṇyandhakavarastriyaḥ 
jagmur ādāya te mlecchāḥ samastā munisattama  ViP 
tataḥ suduḥkhito jiṣṇuḥ kaṣṭaṃ kaṣṭam iti bruvan 
aho bhagavatā tena mukto 'smīti ruroda vai  ViP 
tad dhanus tāni śastrāṇi sa rathas te ca vājinaḥ 
sarvam ekapade naṣṭaṃ dānam aśrotriye yathā  ViP 
aho 'tibalavad daivaṃ vinā tena mahātmanā 
yad asāmarthyayukte 'pi nīcavarge jayapradam  ViP 
tau bāhū sa ca me muṣṭiḥ sthānaṃ tat so 'smi cārjunaḥ 
puṇyenaiva vinā tena gataṃ sarvam asāratām  ViP 
mamārjunatvaṃ bhīmasya bhīmatvaṃ tat kṛtaṃ dhruvam 
vinā tena yad ābhīrair jito 'haṃ katham anyathā  ViP 
parāśara uvāca
itthaṃ vadan yayau jiṣṇur mathurākhyaṃ purottamam 
cakāra tatra rājānaṃ vajraṃ yādavanandanam  ViP 
sa dadarśa tato vyāsaṃ phālgunaḥ kānanāśrayam 
tam upetya mahābhāgaṃ vinayenābhyavādayat  ViP 
taṃ vandamānaṃ caraṇāv avalokya muniś ciram 
uvāca pārthaṃ vicchāyaḥ katham atyantam īdṛśaḥ  ViP 
avīrajo'nugamanaṃ brahmahatyāthavā kṛtā 
dṛḍhāśābhaṅgaduḥkhīva bhraṣṭacchāyo 'si sāmpratam  ViP 
D ins
urjje dattaṃ naiva kṛṣṇe ca pakṣe durvarṇaṃ vā annagodhūmamiśram

agamyastrīratir vā tvaṃ tenāsi vigataprabhaḥ  ViP

kiṃ vā kṛpaṇavittāni hṛtāni bhavatārjuna  ViP

arjuna uvāca
yad balaṃ yac ca nas tejo yad vīryaṃ yaḥ parākramaḥ 
yā śrīś chāyā ca naḥ so 'smān parityajya harir gataḥ  ViP 
itareṇeva mahatā smitapūrvābhibhāṣiṇā 
hīnā vayaṃ mune tena jātās tṛṇamayā iva  ViP 
astrāṇāṃ sāyakānāṃ ca gāṇḍīvasya tathā mama 
sāratā yābhavan mūrtā sa gataḥ puruṣottamaḥ  ViP 
yasyāvalokanād asmāñ śrīr jayaḥ saṃpad unnatiḥ 
na tatyāja sa govindas tyaktvāsmān bhagavān gataḥ  ViP 
bhīṣmadroṇāṅgarājādyās tathā duryodhanādayaḥ 
yatprabhāvena nirdagdhāḥ sa kṛṣṇas tyaktavān bhuvam  ViP 
niryauvanā hataśrīkā bhraṣṭacchāyeva me mahī 
vibhāti tāta naiko 'haṃ virahe tasya cakriṇaḥ  ViP 
yasyānubhāvād bhīṣmādyair mayy agnau śalabhāyitam 
vinā tenādya kṛṣṇena gopālair asmi nirjitaḥ  ViP 
gāṇḍīvaṃ triṣu lokeṣu khyātiṃ yadanubhāvataḥ 
gataṃ tena vinābhīrair laguḍais tannirākṛtam  ViP 
strīsahasrāṇy anekāni mannāthāni mahāmune 
yatato mama nītāni dasyubhir laguḍāyudhaiḥ  ViP 
ānīyamānam ābhīraiḥ kṛṣṇa kṛṣṇāvarodhanam 
hṛtaṃ yaṣṭipraharaṇaiḥ paribhūya balaṃ mama  ViP 
niḥśrīkatā na me citraṃ yaj jīvāmi tad adbhutam 
nīcāvamānapaṅkāṅkī nirlajjo 'smi pitāmaha  ViP

śrīparāśara
atha yogaṃ pravakṣyāmi guhyād guhyataraṃ param  ViP 
yaj jñātvā munayaḥ sarve padaṃ gacchanty anāmayam  ViP 
sāṃkhyāt tattvāt paraṃ yogaṃ pravadanti manīṣiṇaḥ  ViP 
ye yogam anutiṣṭhanti sāṃkhyam apy anutiṣṭate  ViP 
tasmād yogaṃ praśaṃsanti munayo munisattama  ViP 
dehinas tv ātmasaṃyogād yogam āhur manīṣiṇaḥ  ViP 
dehīpāpanibandhatvāt pūrvaṃ pāpakṣayaṃ caret  ViP 
guṇais tu bandhitatvāc ca guṇānāṃ haraṇaṃ tataḥ  ViP 
dehī dehanibandhatvāt tasyāpi haraṇaṃ caret  ViP 
mukhyānāṃ caiva śūnyānāṃ balavattvān niyāmanam  ViP 
evaṃ kṛtvā sma dṛśyantu saṃyojyātmānam ātmani  ViP 
dharmādharmavinirmukto mukta eva bhaved dhruvam  ViP 
guṇānāṃ tejaso rūpaṃ deharūpaṃ ca dehinaḥ  ViP 
ālambya vinaśet paścād yogasiddhim abhīpsatā  ViP 
ālambanān nirālambaṃ paśyanti paramarṣayaḥ  ViP 
ālambanaṃ na cet pūrvaṃ na ca bandhavimokṣaṇam  ViP 
recapūrakakumbhaiś ca pūrvaṃ pāpakṣayaṃ caret  ViP 
pūrvarātralayaiḥ śāntyā dehino dṛśyatāṃ nayet  ViP 
vedasārāt tu saṃyogaṃ pravadanti manīṣiṇaḥ  ViP 
evaṃ yogavidhiḥ prokto yoge sarvaṃ samāpyate  ViP 
evaṃ sāṃkhyaṃ ca yogaṃ ca pravadanti manīṣiṇaḥ  ViP 
anayos tv apṛthagjñānān mukto bhavati nānyathā  ViP

devo nārāyaṇas tv ekaḥ paramātmety udāhṛtaḥ  ViP

bahvākāra ivābhāti māyayā puruṣottamaḥ  ViP 
evaṃ yo veda yogīndraḥ sa vai mukto bhaven naraḥ  ViP

maitreyaḥ

maitreya śrūyatāṃ matto yathāvad upasaṃhṛtiḥ

kaleḥ svarūpaṃ bhagavan vistarād vaktum arhasi

parāśara uvāca

dadyāc ca kāñcanaṃ gāvaś cābhramantaṃ svaśaktitaḥ  ViP 
vācake pūjitaṃ vipra pūjitas tena keśavaḥ  ViP 
kapilādānajanitaṃ puṇyam atyantadurlabham 
śrutvā tv asya daśādhyāyān avāpnoti na saṃśayaḥ  ViP 
yas tvaitat sakalaṃ śṛṇoti puruṣaḥ kṛtvā manasy acyutaṃ sarvaṃ sarvamayaṃ samastajagatām ādhāram ātmāśrayam 
jñānaṃ jñeyam anantam ādirahitaṃ sarvāmarāṇāṃ hitaṃ sa prāpnoti na saṃśayo 'sty avikalaṃ yad vājimedhe phalam  ViP 
yatrādau bhagavāṃś carācaragurur madhye tathānte ca sa brahmajñānamayo 'cyuto 'khilajaganmadhyāntasargaprabhuḥ 
tac chṛṇvan puruṣaḥ pavitraparamaṃ bhaktyā paṭhan dhārayan prāpnoty asti na tat samastabhuvaneṣv ekāntasiddhir hariḥ  ViP 
yasmin nyastamatir na yāti narakaṃ svargo 'pi yac cintane vighno yatra niveśitātmamanaso brāhmo 'pi loko 'lpakaḥ 
muktiṃ cetasi yaḥ sthito 'maladhiyāṃ puṃsāṃ dadāty avyayaḥ kiṃ citraṃ yad aghaṃ prayāti vilayaṃ tatrācyute kīrtite  ViP 
yajñair yajñavido yajanti satataṃ yajñeśvaraṃ karmiṇo yaṃ yaṃ brahmamayaṃ parāparaparaṃ dhyāyanti ca jñāninaḥ 
yaṃ saṃprāpya na jāyate na mriyate no vardhate hīyate naivāsan na ca sad bhavaty ati tataḥ kiṃ vā hareḥ śrūyatām  ViP 
kavyaṃ yaḥ pitṛrūpadhṛg vidhihutaṃ havyaṃ ca bhuṅkte vibhur devatve bhagavān anādinidhanaḥ svāhāsvadhāsaṃjñitaḥ 
yasmin brahmaṇi sarvaśaktinilaye mānāni no mānināṃ niṣṭhāyai prabhavanti hanti kaluṣaṃ śrotraṃ sa yāto hariḥ  ViP 
nānto 'sti yasya na ca yasya samudbhavo 'sti vṛddhir na yasya pariṇāmavivarjitasya 
nāpakṣayaṃ ca samupaity avikalpavastu yas taṃ nato 'smi puruṣottamam īśam īḍyam  ViP 
tasyaiva yo 'nuguṇabhug bahudhaika eva śuddho 'py aśuddha iva mūrtivibhāgabhedaiḥ 
jñānānvitaḥ sakalatattvavibhūtikartā tasmai nato 'smi puruṣāya sadāvyayāya  ViP 
jñānapravṛttiniyamaikyamayāya puṃso bhogapradānapaṭave triguṇātmakāya 
avyākṛtāya bhavabhāvanakāraṇāya vande svarūpabhavanāya sadājarāya  ViP 
After  Ś ins
oṃ namo bhagavate vāsudevāya  ViP 
jitaṃ te puṇḍarīkākṣa namas te viśvabhāvana 
namas te 'stu hṛṣīkeśa mahāpuruṣapūrvaja  ViP 
vyomānilāgnijalabhūracanāmayāya śabdādibhogyaviṣayopanayakṣamāya 
puṃsaḥ samastakaraṇair upakārakāya vyaktāya sūkṣmavimalāya sadā nato 'smi  ViP 
iti vividham ajasya yasya rūpaṃ prakṛtiparātmamayaṃ sanātanasya 
pradiśatu bhagavān aśeṣapuṃsāṃ harir apajanmajarādikāṃ sa siddhim  ViP 
iti śrīviṣṇupurāṇe ṣaṣṭhe 'ṃśe 'ṣṭamo 'dhyāyaḥ
